
1a1(mdo 'grel): */ (/shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i man ngag gi bstan bcos mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan zhes bya ba rje btsun byams pa mgon pos mdzad pa bzhugs so/)
1b1(mdo 'grel): rgya gar skad du/ a b+hi sa ma yA langkA ra nA ma pradz+nyA pA ra mi to pa de sha shAstra kA ri ka /bod skad du/ shes
1b2(mdo 'grel): rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i man ngag gi bstan bcos mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan zhes bya ba'i tshig le'ur byas pa /
1b3(mdo 'grel): sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo/ /nyan thos zhi ba tshol rnams kun shes nyid
1b4(mdo 'grel): kyis nyer zhir khrid mdzad gang yin dang/ /'gro la phan par byed rnams lam shes nyid kyis 'jig rten don sgrub mdzad pa
2a1(mdo 'grel): gang/ /gang dang yang dag ldan pas thub rnams rnam pa kun ldan sna tshogs 'di gsungs pa/ /nyan thos byang chub
2a2(mdo 'grel): sems dpa' i tshogs bcas sangs rgyas kyi ni yum de la phyag 'tshal lo/ /rnam pa thams cad mkhyen nyid lam/ /ston pas 'di
2a3(mdo 'grel): las bshad pa gang/ /gzhan gyis myong ba ma yin te/ /chos spyod bcu yi bdag nyid kyi/ /mdo don dran pa la bzhag nas/ /blo
2a4(mdo 'grel): dang ldan pas mthong 'gyur phyir/ /bde blag tu ni rtogs pa zhes/ /bya ba rtsom pa'i dgos pa yin/ /shes rab pha rol phyin pa ni//
2b1(mdo 'grel): dngos po brgyad kyis yang dag bshad/ /rnam kun mkhyen nyid lam shes nyid/ /de nas thams cad shes pa nyid/ /rnam kun mngon rdzogs rtogs
2b2(mdo 'grel): pa dang/ /rtse mor phyin dang mthar gyis pa/ /skad cig gcig mngon rdzogs byang chub/ /chos kyi sku dang de rnam brgyad/ /sems bskyed pa dang gdams
2b3(mdo 'grel): ngag dang/ /nges 'byed yan lag rnam bzhi dang/ /sgrub pa yi ni rten gyur pa/ /chos kyi dbyings kyi rang bzhin dang/ /dmigs pa dag dang ched dang ni/ /
2b4(mdo 'grel): go cha 'jug pa'i bya ba dang/ /tshogs ni nges par 'byung bcas rnams/ /thub pa'i rnam kun mkhyen pa nyid/ /mog mog por byed la sogs dang//
2b5(mdo 'grel): slob ma bse ru'i lam gang dang/ /'di dang gzhan pa'i yon tan gyis/ /phan yon che ba mthong ba'i lam/ /byed pa dang ni mos pa dang/ /bstod dang
3a1(mdo 'grel): bkur dang bsngags pa dang/ /bsngo dang rjes su yi rang ba/ /yid la byed pa bla med dag /sgrub dang shin tu dag pa zhes/ /bya ba 'di ni sgom pa'i
3a2(mdo 'grel): lam/ /byang chub sems dpa' mkhas rnams kyi/ /lam shes nyid ni de 'drar bshad/ /shes pas srid pa mi gnas shing/ /snying rjes zhi la mi gnas
3a3(mdo 'grel): dang/ /thabs ma yin pas ring ba dang/ /thabs kyis ring ba ma yin nyid/ /mi mthun gnyen po'i phyogs dag dang/ /sbyor dang de yi mnyam nyid dang/ /nyan thos
3a4(mdo 'grel): la sogs mthong ba'i lam/ /de 'dra kun shes nyid du 'dod/ /rnam pa sbyor bar bcas rnams dang/ /yon tan skyon ni mtshan nyid bcas/ /thar dang nges 'byed
3a5(mdo 'grel): cha mthun dang/ /slob pa phyir mi ldog pa'i tshogs/ /srid dang zhi ba mnyam nyid dang/ /zhing dag bla na med pa ni/ /rnam kun mngon rdzogs rtogs pa ste//
3b1(mdo 'grel): 'di ni thabs mkhas bcas pa yin/ /de yi rtags dang rnam 'phel dang/ /brtan dang sems kun gnas pa dang/ /mthong zhes bya dang sgom pa zhes/ /bya ba'i lam ni so so la/ /rnam par rtog
3b2(mdo 'grel): pa rnam bzhi yi/ /gnyen po rnam pa bzhi dang ni/ /bar chad med pa'i ting nge 'dzin/ /log par bsgrub dang bcas pa ni/ /rtse mo'i mngon rtogs mthar gyis pa/ /rnam gsum rnam bcu skad cig ma/ /
3b3(mdo 'grel): gcig gis mngon rdzogs byang chub pa/ /mtshan nyid kyis ni rnam pa bzhi/ /ngo bo nyid longs rdzogs bcas dang/ /de bzhin gzhan pa sprul pa ni/ /chos sku mdzad pa dang bcas pa/ /rnam pa bzhir
3b4(mdo 'grel): ni yang dag brjod/ /sems bskyed pa ni gzhan don phyir/ /yang dag rdzogs pa'i byang chub 'dod/ /de dang de ni mdo bzhin du/ /bsdus dang rgyas pa'i sgo nas brjod/ /de yang sa gser zla ba
3b5(mdo 'grel): me/ /gter dang rin chen 'byung gnas mtsho/ /rdo rje ri sman bshes gnyen dang/ /yid bzhin nor bu nyi ma glu/ /rgyal po mdzod dang lam po che/ /gzhon pa bkod ma'i chu dang ni/ /sgra
3b6(mdo 'grel): snyan chu bo sprin rnams kyis/ /rnam pa nyi shu rtsa gnyis so/ /sgrub dang bden pa rnams dang ni/ /sangs rgyas la sogs dkon mchog gsum/ /ma zhen yongs su mi ngal dang//
4a1(mdo 'grel): lam ni yongs su 'dzin pa dang/ /spyan lnga dang ni mngon shes kyi/ /yon tan drug dang mthong lam dang/ /sgom zhes bya la gdams ngag ni/ /bcu yi bdag nyid shes par bya/ /
4a2(mdo 'grel): dbang po rtul dang rnon po dag /dad dang mthong thob rigs nas rigs/ /bar chad gcig par skyes nas dang/ /byed dang byed min 'og min 'gro/ /'phar gsum srid rtse'i mthar thug 'gro/ /
4a3(mdo 'grel): gzugs kyi chags bcom mthong ba yi/ /chos la zhi lus mngon sum byed/ /bse ru dang ni nyi shu'o/ /dmigs pa dang ni rnam pa dang/ /rgyu dang yongs su 'dzin pa dang/ /byang chub sems
4a4(mdo 'grel): dpa' skyob pa yi/ /drod sogs bdag nyid ji bzhin du/ /rnam rtog bzhi po ldan bsten pa/ /chung dang 'bring dang chen po rnams/ /nyan thos bse ru lta bu dang/ /bcas pa dag las khyad par 'phags//
4a5(mdo 'grel): dmigs pa mi rtag la sogs pa/ /bden pa'i rten can de yi ni/ /rnam pa mngon zhen la sogs 'gog /theg pa gsum car 'thob pa'i rgyu/ /gzugs sogs 'du 'god gnas bral dang/ /gnas dang btags dang brjod du
4a6(mdo 'grel): med/ /gzugs sogs mi gnas de dag ni/ /de yi ngo bo rang bzhin med/ /de dag gcig gi rang bzhin gcig /de mi rtags sogs bar mi gnas/ /de rnams de yi ngo bos stong/ /de dag gcig gi rang bzhin gcig/ chos rnams mi 'dzin gang yin dang//
4b1(mdo 'grel): de dag mtshan mar mi mthong phyir/ /shes rab kyis ni yongs rtog pa/ /thams cad dmigs su med par ro/ /gzugs sogs ngo bo nyid med nyid/ /de med pa nyid ngo bo nyid/ /de dag skye med nges 'byung med/ /dag dang de dag mtshan ma med/ /de yi
4b2(mdo 'grel): mtshan mar mi brten pas/ /mos min 'du shes med pa yin/ /ting 'dzin de yi byed pa nyid/ /lung ston pa dang rlom pa zad/ /gsum po phan tshun ngo bo gcig /ting 'dzin rnam par mi rtog pa/ /de ltar nges 'byes cha mthun ni/ /chung dang 'bring dang chen po
4b3(mdo 'grel): yin/ /gzhi dang de yi gnyen po yis/ /gzung bar rtog pa rnam pa gnyis/ /rmongs dang phung sogs bye brag gis/ /de ni so sor rnam pa dgu /rdzas dang btags pa'i rten can gyis/ /'dzin pa'ang rnam pa gnyis su 'dod/ /rang dbang bdag sogs ngo bo dang/
4b4(mdo 'grel): phung sogs rten las de bzhin no/ /sems mi 'gong ba nyid la sogs/ /ngo bo nyid med sogs ston byed/ /de yi mi mthun phyogs bor pa/ /rnam pa kun tu yongs 'dzin yin/ /rtogs pa yi ni chos drug dang/ /gnyen po dang ni spong ba dang/ /de dag yongs
4b5(mdo 'grel): su gtugs pa dang/ /shes rab snying brtser bcas pa dang/ /slob ma thun mong min nyid dang/ /gzhan gyi don gyi go rim dang/ /ye shes rtsol ba mi mnga' bar/ /'jug pa'i rten la rigs zhes bya/ /chos kyi dbyings la dbyer med phyir/ /rigs ni tha dang rung ma
4b6(mdo 'grel): yin/ /brten pa'i chos kyi bye brag gis/ /de yi dbye ba yongs su brjod/ /dmigs pa chos rnams thams cad de/ /de yang dge la sogs pa yin/ /'jig rten pa yi rtogs pa dang/ /gang dag 'jig rten 'das 'dod dang/ /zag bcas zag pa med chos dang/
4b7(mdo 'grel): gang dag 'dus byas 'dus ma byas/ /slob ma thun mong chos rnams dang/ /gang dag thub pa'i thun mong min/ /sems can kun mchog nyid sems dang/ /spong dang rtogs dang gsum po la/ /chen po gsum po rang byung gi /ched du bya ba 'di shes bya/ /de dag so
5a1(mdo 'grel): sor sbyin la sogs/ /rnam pa drug tu bsdus pa yis/ /cho ga'i sgrub pa gang yin de/ /drug tshan drug gis ji bzhin bshad/ /bsam gtan gzugs med sbyin sogs dang/ /lam dang byams la sogs pa dang/ /dmigs pa
5a2(mdo 'grel): med dang ldan pa dang/ /bsor gsum rnam par dag pa dang/ /ched du bya dang mngon shes drug /rnam kun mkhyen pa'i tshul la ni/ /'jug pa'i sgrub pa theg chen la/ /'dzeg pa yin par shes par bya/ /brtse dang sbyin la sogs pa drug/ zhi gnas lhag
5a3(mdo 'grel): mthong bcas pa dang/ /zung du 'brel ba'i lam gang dang/ /thabs la mkhas pa gang yin dang/ /ye shes dang ni bsod nams dang/ /lam dang gzung dang sa bcu dang/ /gnyen po'i tshogs kyi sgrub pa yi/ /rim pa yin par shes par bya/ /yongs su
5a4(mdo 'grel): sbyong ba rnam bcu yis/ /sa ni dang po 'thob 'gyur te/ /bsam dang phan pa'i dngos nyid dang/ /sems can rnams la sems mnyam nyid/ /gtod dang bshes gnyen bsten pa dang/ /dam chos dmigs pa tshol ba dang/ /rtag tu des 'byung sems nyid dang//
5a5(mdo 'grel): sangs rgyas bkur 'dod dga' ba dang/ /chos ston pa dang bden pa yi/ /tshig ni bcu pa yin par 'dod/ /'di dag rang bzhin mi dmigs pas/ /yongs su sbyong bar shes par bya/ /tshul khrims byas pa gzo dang bzod/ /rab tu dga' dang snying brtse che/ /
5a6(mdo 'grel): bkur sti bla ma la gus nyan/ /brgyad pa sbyin pa sogs la brtson/ /thos pas mi ngoms nyid dang ni/ /zang zing med par chos sbyin dang/ /sangs rgyas zhing kun sbyor ba dang/ /'khor bas yongs su mi skyo dang/ /ngo tsha khrel yod ces bya ba/ /rlom med bdag nyid
5a7(mdo 'grel): de rnam lnga/ /nags gnas 'dod chung chog shes dang/ /spyangs pa yang dag sdom sten dang/ /bslab pa yongs su mi gtong dang/ /'dod pa rnams la smyong ba dang/ /mya ngan 'das dang bdog kun gtod/ /rmi zhum pa dang lhab med/ /'dris dang khyim la 'khren pa dang
5b1(mdo 'grel): 'du 'dzir gyur pa'i gnas dang ni/ /bdag bstod gzhan la brnyas ba dang/ /mi dge'i las kyi lam bcu dang/ /rlom pas khengs dang phyin ci log /blo ngan dang ni nyon mongs bzod/ /bcu po 'di ni rnam spangs nas/ /sa lnga pa ni yang dag 'thob/ /sbyin dang tshul khrims
5b2(mdo 'grel): bzod brtson 'grus/ /bsam gtan shes rab rab rdzogs pas/ /slob ma dang ni bse ru la/ /dga' dang skrag pa'i sems spangs pa/ /bslangs na mi zhum bdog pa kun/ /btang yang mi dga' med pa dang/ /dbul yang slong ba mi spong bas/ /sa ni drug pa yang dag
5b3(mdo 'grel): 'thob/ /bdag dang sems can 'dzin pa dang/ /srog dang gang zag chad rtag dang/ /mtshan ma rgyu dang phung po dang/ /khams dang skye mched dag dang ni/ /khams gsum pa la gnas dang chags/ /sems ni kun tu zhum pa dang/ /dkon mchog gsum dang tshul khrims
5b4(mdo 'grel): la/ /der lta ba yi mngon zhen dang/ /stong pa nyid la rtsod pa dang/ /de dang 'gal ba'i nyes pa ni/ /nyi shu gang la rnam chad pa/ /de yis sa ni bdun pa 'thob/ /rnam thar sgo gsum shes pa dang/ /'khor gsum rnam pa bdag nyid dang/ /snying rje dang ni rlom med dang/ /chos
5b5(mdo 'grel): mnyam nyid dang tshul gcig shes/ /mi skye ba dang bzod shes dang/ /chos rnams rnam pa gcig tu ston/ /rtog pa kun tu 'joms pa dang/ /'du shes lta dang nyon mongs spong/ /zhi gnas nges par sems pa dang/ lhag mthong la ni mkhas pa dang/ /sems dul
5b6(mdo 'grel): ba dang thams cad la/ /thogs ba med pa'i ye shes dang/ /chags pa'i sa min gang 'dod par/ /zhing gzhan du ni mnyam 'gro dang/ /kun tu bdag gi ngo bo ni/ /ston pa nyid dang nyi shu'o/ /sems can kun yid shes pa dang/ /mngon par shes pas brtse ba
5b7(mdo 'grel): dang/ /sangs rgyas zhing bzab bsgrub pa dang/ /yongs su brtag phyir sangs rgyas bsten/ /dbang po shes dang rgyal ba yi/ /zhing spyong sgyu ma ltar gnas dang/ /bsams bzhin sred pa len pa dang/ /las ni rnam pa 'di brgyad bshad/ /smon lam dag ni
6a1(mdo 'grel): mdza' yas dang/ /lha la sogs pa'i skad shes dang/ /spobs pa chu bo lta bu dang/ /mngal du 'jug pa mchog dang ni/ /rigs dang rus dang cho 'bring dang/ /'khor dang skye ba dag dang ni/ /des 'byung byang chub shing rnams dang/ /yon
6a2(mdo 'grel): tan phun sum tshogs pa yin/ /sa dgu 'das nas ye shes ni/ /gang gis sangs rgyas sar gnas pa/ /de ni byang chub sems dpa' i sa/ /bcu pa yin par shes par bya/ /mthong dang goms pa'i lam dag la/ gzung dang 'dzin pa'i rnam rtog rnams/
6a3(mdo 'grel): nye bar zhi bar bya ba'i phyir/ /gnyen po rnam pa brgyad ces bya/ /ched du bya dang mnyam nyid dang/ /sems can don dang 'bang med dang/ /mdza' las 'das par nges 'byung dang/ /thob pa'i mtshan nyid nges 'byung dang/ /rnam pa thams cad mkhyen nyid dang//
6a4(mdo 'grel): lam gyi yul can nges 'byung ste/ rnam pa brgyad kyi bdag nyid 'di/ /nges 'byung sgrub pa yin zhes bya/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i man ngag gi bstan bcos mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan gyi tshig le'ur byas pa las/ skabs dang po'o// //
6a5(mdo 'grel): lha rnams rung bar bya ba'i phyir/ /'od kyis mog mog por mdzad dang/ /yul nges pa dang khyab pa dang/ /rang bzhin dang ni de yi las/ /lam shes nyid kyi tshul la ni/ 'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi dag gi /rnam pa mi dmigs sgo nas ni/ /nyan thos lam 'di shes par bya
6a6(mdo 'grel): 'phags pa nyan thos lam la ni/ /gzugs la sogs pa stong pa'i phyir/ /stong pa nyid rnams dbyer med pas/ /dro ba de dag mi dmigs pas/ /rtse mor gyur pa dag tu 'dor/ /de la rtag la sogs tshul gyis/ /gnas pa bkag pas bzod pa rnams/ /sa bcu dag las brtsams
6a7(mdo 'grel): nas ni/ /mi gnas rgyas par bstan pa yis/ /chos kyi mchog tu 'gyur bshad de/ /ci phyir zhe na sangs rgyas kyis/ /mkhyen nas chos rnams ma gzigs phyir/ /rang byung bdag nyid rtogs pa'i phyir/ /gzhan gyis bstan yang mi dgos la/ /bse ru lta bu'i ye shes ni/ zang
6b1(mdo 'grel): pa nyid ru mngon par brjod/ /gang gang don ni gang gang la/ /ji lta ji ltar nyan 'dod pa/ /de de la don de dang de/ /sgra med kyang de de ltar snang/ /gzung don rtog pa spong phyir dang/ /'dzin pa mi spong phyir dang ni/ rten gyis bsu ru lta bu'i lam/ /yang dag bsdus par
6b2(mdo 'grel): shes bar bya/ /btags pa'i chos nyid mi 'gal bar/ ston pa'i rnam pa dror gyur ba/ /rtse mor gyur pa gzugs la sogs/ /'grib pa med la sogs pas phye/ nang stong nyid la sogs pa yis/ /gzugs sogs mi 'dzin phyir bzod pa/ /gzugs sogs skye ba med sogs kyi/ rnam
6b3(mdo 'grel): pa can ni chos kyi mchog /bden dang bden la bzod pa dang/ /shes pa'i skad cig rnam bzhi yis/ /lam shes nyid la mthong ba'i lam/ /phan yon bcas pa 'di bshad do/ /de bzhin nyid dang sangs rgyas dag /phan tshun brten pa rten med phyir/ /rnam grangs khas mi len pa dang/ /chen
6b4(mdo 'grel): po tshad ma med bcas dang/ /tshad med pa dang mthab med dang/ /der gnas gzugs la sogs pa la/ /sangs rgyas nyid du nges 'dzin dang/ /blang med dor ba med sogs dang/ /byams la sogs dang stong nyid dang/ /sangs rgyas nyid ni 'thob pa dang/ /rnam par byad kun yongs bsdus dang//
6b5(mdo 'grel): nyam nga ba dang nang kun sel/ /mya ngan 'das 'dzin zhi nyid dang/ /sangs rgyas rnams kyis bsrung la sogs/ /srog mi gcod pa la sogs pa/ /rnam pa kun mkhyen tshul la ni/ /bdag nyid gnas te sems can dag /'gong dang sbyin pa la sogs pa/ /rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu bsngo ba/ /
6b6(mdo 'grel): lam shes nyid kyi skad cig ma/ /kun nas zhi dang thams cad la/ /bdud dang nyon mongs las rgyal dang/ /gnod pas brdzi ba med nyid dang/ /byang chub dang ni rten mchod nyid/ mos pa rang gi don dang ni/ /rang gzhan don dang gzhan don dang/ rnam gsum shes bya de yang ni/ /chung dang 'bring
6b7(mdo 'grel): dang chen po ste/ /so sor rnam pa gsum du 'dod/ /chung ngu'i chung sogs dbye ba yis/ /de yang rnam gsum de ltar na/ rnam pa nyi shu bdun du 'dod/ shes rab pha rol phyin pa la/ /mos pa'i gnas skabs rnams la ni/ /dgu tshan gsum gyis bstod pa dang/ /bkur ba dang ni bsngags
7a1(mdo 'grel): yang 'dod/ /yongs su bsngo ba khyad par can/ /de yi byed pa mchog yin no/ /de ni dmigs med rnam pa can/ /phyin ci ma log mtshan nyid do/ /dben dang sangs rgyas bsod nams tshogs/ /rang bzhin dran pa'i spyod yul can/ /thabs bcas mtshan ma med pa dang/
7a2(mdo 'grel): sangs rgyas rjes su yi rang dang/ /khams gsum gtogs pa ma yin dang/ /chung dang 'bring dang chen po yi/ /bsngo ba gzhan ni rnam gsum po/ /bsod nams che 'byung bdag nyid do/ /thabs dang mi dmigs pa dag gis/ dge ba'i rtsa la yi rang ba/ /rjes su yi rang yid
7a3(mdo 'grel): byed pa/ /sgom pa yin par 'dir brjod do/ /de yi ngo bo nyid mchog nyid/ /kun la mngon par 'du mi byed/ /chos rnams dmigs su med par ni/ /gtong par byed pa don chen nyid/ /sangs rgyas bsten dang sbyin sogs dang/ /thabs la mkhas pa gang yin pa/ /'di la mos
7a4(mdo 'grel): pa'i rgyu dag yin/ /chos kyi phongs pa'i rgyu dag ni/ /bdud kyi thibs kyis non pa dang/ /zab mo'i chos la ma mos dang/ /phung po la sogs mngon zhen dang/ /sdig pa'i grogs pos yongs zin pa'o/ /'bras bu dag pa gzugs la sogs/ /dag pa nyid de gang gi phyir/ /de gnyis
7a5(mdo 'grel): tha dad ma yin zhing/ /bcad du med pas dag par brjod/ /nyon mongs shes bya lam gsum gyi/ /nyams phyir slob ma bse ru dang/ /rgyal sras rnams kyi dag pa ste/ /sangs rgyas rnam kun shin tu ba/ /sa dgu la ni chen po yi/ /chen po la sogs dri ma yi/ /gnyen po
7a6(mdo 'grel): chung ngu'i chung ngu la/ /sogs pa'i lam ni dag pa yin/ /de la klan ka spangs pa yis/ /lam ni 'jal dang gzhal bya dag /mnyam pa nyid kyis khams gsum gyi/ /gnyen po nyid du 'dod pa yin/ /shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i man ngag gi bstan bcos mngon
7a7(mdo 'grel): par rtogs pa'i rgyan gyi tshig le'ur byas pa las/ skabs gnyis pa'o// //chu rol pha rol mdza' la min/ /de dag par na mi gnas pa/ /dus rnams mnyam pa nyid shes phyir/ shes rab pha rol phyin par 'dod/ /de ni mtshan mar dmigs sgo nas/ /thabs ma
7b1(mdo 'grel): yin pas ring bas te/ /de ni thabs la mkhas pa yis/ /yang dag nye ba nyid du bshad/ /gzugs sogs phung po stong nyid dang/ /dus gsum gtogs pa'i chos rnams dang/ /spyin sogs byang chub phyogs rnams la/ /spyod pa'i 'du shes mi mthun phyogs/ /sbyin la sogs
7b2(mdo 'grel): la ngar 'dzin med/ /gzhan dag de la sbyor byed pa/ /de ni tshags pa'i mdza' 'gog pas/ /rgyal la sogs la chags pa phra/ /chos kyi lam ni rang bzhin gyis/ /dben pa'i phyir na de zab nyid/ /chos rnams rang bzhin gcig par ni/ /shes pas chags pa spong ba yin/ /mthong ba la
7b3(mdo 'grel): sogs bkag pa yis/ /de ni rtogs par dka' bar bshad/ /gzugs la sogs par mi shes phyir/ /de ni bsam mi khyab par 'dod/ /de ltar kun shes nyid lugs la/ /mi mthun gnyen po'i phyogs dag gi /rnam par dbye ba ma lus pa/ /ji skad bshad pa 'dir shes bya/ /gzugs
7b4(mdo 'grel): sogs de mi rtag sogs dang/ /de ma rdzogs dang rab rdzogs dang/ /de la chags pa med nyid la/ /spyod pa bkag pa'i sbyor ba dang/ /mi 'gyur ?? po med nyid dang/ /bya bka' rnam gsum sbyor ba dang/ /skal pa ji bzhin 'bras thob pas/ /'bras yod 'dod pa de dang ni/ /gzhan la rag las
7b5(mdo 'grel): med gang dang/ /snang ba rnam bdun shes byed do/ /gzugs la sogs la rlom med pa/ /rnam bzhi de yi mnyam pa nyid/ /sdug bsngal la sogs bden pa la/ /chos shes rjes su shes pa dang/ /bzod shes skad cig bdag nyid 'di/ /kun shes tshul la mthong ba'i lam/ /gzugs rtag
7b6(mdo 'grel): ma yin mi rtag min/ /mdza' las 'das dang rnam dag dang/ /ma skyes ma 'gags la sogs dang/ /mkha' 'dra chags pa spangs pa dang/ /yongs su 'dzin las grol ba dang/ /ngo bo nyid kyis brjod med dang/ /gang phyir 'di don brjod pa yis/ /gzhan la sbyin du med pa dang/ /dmigs pa
7b7(mdo 'grel): med par byed pa dang/ /shin tu rnam dag med mi 'byung ngo/ /ngan song ? dang 'bras bu ni/ /mngon du bya la mi rtog nyid/ /mtshan ma dag dang ma 'brel dang/ /dngos dang ming dang gnyis po la/ /shes ba skye ba med pa ni/ /kun shes nyid kyi skad cig ma/ /de ltar 'di dang yang 'di dang/ /yang
8a1(mdo 'grel): 'di yin te rnam gsum po/ /'di ni gnas skabs gsum po dag /rdzogs par yongs su bstan pa yin/ /shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i man ngag gi bsnyan bcos mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan gyi tshig le'ur byas pa las/ skabs gsum
8a2(mdo 'grel): pa'o// //gzhi shes pa yi bye brag rnams/ /rnam pa zhes bya mtshan nyid de/ /kun mkhyen nyid ni rnam gsum phyir/ /de ni rnam pa gsum du 'dod/ /med pa'i rnam pa nas bzung ste/ /mi g.yo ba yi rnam pa'i bar/ /bden pa so so la bzhi dang/ /lam
8a3(mdo 'grel): la de ni bco lngar bshad/ /rgyu dang lam dang sdug bsngal dang/ /'gog pa la ni go rim bzhin/ /de dag brgyad dang bdun dang ni/ /lnga dang bcu drug ces bsgrags so/ /dran pa nyer gzhag nas gzung ste/ /sangs rgyas rnam pa'i mthar thug rnams/ lam gyi bden pa'i rjes mthun
8a4(mdo 'grel): par/ /kun mkhyen gsum du phye bas na/ /slob ma byang chub sems dpa' dang/ /sangs rgyas rnams la rim bzhin de/ /sum cu bdun dang sum cu bzhi/ /sum cu rtsa dgu dag tu bzhed/ /sangs rgyas rnams la lhag par byas/ /de la dge ba'i rtsa ba bskrun/ /dge ba'i bshes kyi
8a5(mdo 'grel): mgon bcas pa/ /'di mnyan pa yi snod yin no/ /sangs rgyas bsten dang kun 'dri dang/ /sbyin dang tshul khrims sogs spyod pas/ /len dang 'dzin pa la sogs pa'i/ /snod du dam pa rnams bzhed do/ /gzugs la sogs la mi gnas phyir/ /de la sbyor ba bkag pa'i phyir//
8a6(mdo 'grel): de yi de bzhin nyid zab phyir/ /de rnams gting dpag dka' ba'i phyir/ /de dag tshad ni med phyir dang/ /tshegs chen yun ring rtogs pa'i phyir/ /lung bstan phyir mi ldog nyid dang/ /nges 'byung bar chad med bcas dang/ /byang chub nye dang myur ba dang/ /gzhan don 'phel med 'grib
8a7(mdo 'grel): med phyir/ /chos dang chos min sogs mi mthong/ /gzugs sogs bsam mi khyab mi mthong/ /gzugs sogs de yi mtshan ma dang/ /de yi ngo bo rnam mi rtog /'bras bu rin chen sbyin byed dang/ /de ni dag pa mtshams dang bcas/ /bdud kyi mthu bcom la sogs pa/
8b1(mdo 'grel): yon tan rnam pa bcu bzhi'o/ /skyon ni bcu mtshan bzhir bcas pa/ /drug tu nges par rtogs par bya/ /gang gis mtshon te mtshan nyid tu/ /shes bya de yang rnam pa gsum/ /shes pa khyad par byed pa ste/ /ngo bo nyid gang mtshon bya yang/ /de bzhin gshegs pa 'gyur ro/?
8b2(mdo 'grel): 'jig rten 'jig med bdag nyid dang/ /sems can sems kyi spyod pa dang/ /de bsdus pa dang phyir ltas dang/ /mi zad pa yi rnam pa dang/ /chags bcas sogs dang rgya chen dang/ /chen por gyur dang tshad med dang/ /rnam shes bstan du med pa dang/ /sems bltar med dang shes pa
8b3(mdo 'grel): de/ /g.yo ba la sogs shes bya dang/ /de las gzhan yang de dag ni/ /de bzhin nyid kyi rnam par shes/ /thub pas de bzhin nyid rtogs te/ /gzhan la bstan pa zhes bya 'di/ /thams cad shes pa nyid skabs kyi/ /shes pa'i mtshan nyid bsdus pa yin/ /stong nyid mtshan ma med
8b4(mdo 'grel): bcas dang/ /smon pa rnam par spangs pa dang/ /skye med 'gag pa med sogs dang/ /chos nyid rnam par 'khrug med dang/ /'du mi byed dang rnam mi rtog /rab dbye mtshan nyid med nyid la/ /lam shes nyid kyi skabs kyis ni/ /shes pa'i mtshan nyid yin par bzhed/ /de
8b5(mdo 'grel): ni nyid kyi chos bsten nas/ /gnas dang gus par bya ba dang/ /bla ma nyid dang mnyes pa dang/ /de la mchod dang byang med dang/ /kun tu 'jug mkhyen gang yin dang/ ma mthong ston par mdzad pa dang/ /'jig rten stong nyid rnam pa dang/ /brjod dang shes mdzad mngon
8b6(mdo 'grel): sum mdzad/ /bsam mi khyab dang zhi nyid ston/ /'jig rten 'du shes 'gog pa la/ /rnam pa kun mkhyen tshul la ni/ /shes pa'i mtshan nyid ces bshad do/ /bsam mi khyab sogs khyad par gyis/ /khyad zhugs bden pa'i spyod yul can/ /skad cig ma ni bcu
8b7(mdo 'grel): drug gis/ /khyad par mtshan nyid bshad pa yin/ /bsam mi khyab dang mi mnyam dang/ /gzhal dang bgrang las yang dag 'das?/ /'phags pa kun sdud mkhas pa yis/ rig bya thun mong min shes nyid/ /shes myur bri dang gang med dang/ /sgrub dang yang dag 'grub
9a1(mdo 'grel): pa dang/ /dmigs pa rten dang bcas pa dang/ /mdza' dag pa dang yongs 'dzin dang/ /ro myang med dang khyad par ni/ /bcu drug bdag nyid ces bya ste/ /gang gis lam ni gzhan dag las/ /khyad du 'phags pas khyad par lam/ /phan dang bde dang
9a2(mdo 'grel): skyob pa dang/ /mi rnams kyi ni skyabs dag dang/ /gnas dang dbung gnyen gling dang ni/ /yongs 'dren pa zhes bya ba dang/ lhun gyis grub dang theg gsum gyi/ /'bras bu mngon sum mi byed dag/ /tha ma rten gyi mdzad pa ste/ /'di ni byed pa'i mtshan nyid yin/ /nyon
9a3(mdo 'grel): mongs rtags dang mtshan ma dang/ /mi mthun phyogs dang gnyen mo dag/ dben dang dka' dang nges pa dang/ /ched du bya dang mi dmigs dang/ /mngon par zhen pa bkag pa dang/ /dmigs pa zhes bya gang yin dang/ /mi mthun thogs pa med dang de/ /gzhi me
9a4(mdo 'grel): 'gro med skye med dang/ /de bzhin nyid ni mi dmigs dang/ /ngo bo nyid bcu drug bdag nyid/ /mtshon bya lta bur mtshon pas na/ /mtshan nyid bzhi par bzhed pa yin/ /mtshan med rab tu sbyin la sogs/ /yang dag sgrub la mkhas pa ni/ /rnam pa thams
9a5(mdo 'grel): cad rtogs 'di la/ /thar pa'i cha dang mthun par 'dod/ /sangs rgyas sogs dmigs dad pa dang/ /sbyin sogs spyod yul brtson 'grus dang/ /bsam pa phun tshogs dran pa dang/ /rnam par mi rtog ting 'dzin dang/ /chos rnams rnam pa thams cad du//
9a6(mdo 'grel): shes pa'i shes rab dang rnam lnga/ /rdzogs pa'i byang chub rnon po yis/ /rtogs bla rtul pos rtogs dkar bzhed/ /dro ba rnams kyi dmigs pa 'dir/ /sems can thams cad yin par bsngags/ /de dag nyid la sems mnyam sogs/ /rnam pa dag ni bcur
9a7(mdo 'grel): bshad do/ /bdag nyid sdig pa las ldog cing/ /sbyin la sogs pa gnas pas gzhan/ /de dag la ni 'god pa dang/ /bsngags pa brjod dang mthun pa nyid/ /brtser gyur de bzhin bzod pa ni/ /rang gzhan rten can bden shes pa/ /chos mchog de bzhin sems can rnams//
9b1(mdo 'grel): smin byed sogs kyis shes bar bya/ /nges 'byed yan lag nas bzung ste/ /mthong dang goms pa'i lam dag la/ /byang chub sems dpa' gang dag gnas/ /de 'dir phyir mi ldog pa'i tshogs/ /gzugs la sogs las ldog sogs rtags/ /rnam pa nyi shur brjod pa?  /
9b2(mdo 'grel): nges 'byed yan lag la gnas pa'i/ /phyir mi ldog pa'i mtshan nyid 'di/ /gzugs la sogs las ldog pa dang/ the tshom mi ngal zad pa dang/ /bdag nyid dge ba la gnas shing/ /gzhan dag de la 'god pa dang/ /gzhan gyi rten can sbyin sogs dang/ /zab mo'i don
9b3(mdo 'grel): la'ang? som nyi med/ /byams lus sogs dang sgrib pa ni/ /rnam pa lnga dang mi 'grogs dang/ /bag la nyal kun 'joms pa dang/ /dran pa dang ni shes bzhin dang/ /gos la sogs pa gtsang ba dang/ /lus la srin bu rnams mi 'byung/ /gya gyu med sems sbyangs pa ni/ /len dang
9b4(mdo 'grel): ser sna med sogs dang/ /chos nyid ldan par 'gro nyid dang/ sems can don du myal tshol dang/ /gzhal gyis bkri bar mi btub dang/ /lam gzhan nye bar ston bdud la/ /bdud ces bya bar rtogs pa dang/ /sangs rgyas dgyes pa'i spyod pa ste/ /rtags ni nyi shu de dag gis/ /
9b5(mdo 'grel): drod dang rtse mo bzod bcas dang/ /chos mchog rnams la gnas pa ni/ /rdzogs pa'i byang chub las mi ldog/ mthong ba'i lam la bzod pa dang/ /shes pa'i skad cig bcu drug ni/ /byang chub sems dpa' mi ldog pa'i/ /mtshan nyid yin par shes par bya/ /gzugs sogs 
9b6(mdo 'grel): ba'u shes ldog pa dang/ /sems brtan theg pa dman dag las/ /rnam log bsam gtan la sogs pa'i/ /yan lag yongs su zad pa dang/ /lus sems yang ba nyid dang ni/ /'dod pa sbyod la thabs mkhas dang/ /rtag tu tshang par sbyod nyid dang/ /'tsho ba rnam par dag nyid
9b7(mdo 'grel): 'ang/ /gung sogs bar chad byed rnams dang/ /tshogs dang dbang sogs bcas pa yi/ /g.yul 'gyed ser sna la sogs la/ /sbyor dang rjes su sbyor ba yi/ /gnas pa so sor bkag pa dang/ /chos ni rdul tsam mi dmigs nyid/ /rang gi sa la nges pa nyid/ /sa gsum la ni gnas pa
10a1(mdo 'grel): dang/ /chos kyi don du srog gtong ba/ /de 'dra'i skad cig bcu drug ni/ /blo ldan mthong ba'i lam gnas kyi/ /phyir mi ldog pa'i rtag dag yin/ /sgom pa'i lam ni zab pa ste/ /zab mo stong pa nyid la sogs/ /zab pa de ni sgro 'dogs dang/ /skur ba'i
10a2(mdo 'grel): mdza' las grol ba nyid/ /nges 'byed yan lag dang mthong ba'i/ /lam dang sgom pa'i lam nyid la/ yang dang yang du sems pa dang/ /'byal dang nges rtog gi sgom pa'i lam/ /de ni rgyun chags yin pa'i phyir/ /chung dang 'bring dang chen po rnams/ /chung ngu'i chung sogs bye
10a3(mdo 'grel): ba yis/ /rnam pas rnam pa dgur bzhed do/ /grangs med la sogs bsten bsten pa rnams/ /dam pa'i don du bzod ma yin/ /kun rdzob tu ni thugs brtse ba'i/ /rgyu mthun de dag thub pa bzhed/ /dngos po brjod du med pa la/ /nyams pa dang ni 'phel mi rung/ /sgom zhes bya
10a4(mdo 'grel): ba'i lam gyis ni/ /ci zhig nyams shing ci zhig 'thob/ /byang chub ji lta de bzhin du/ /'di ni 'dod pa'i don sgrub byed/ /byang chub de bzhin nyid mtshan nyid/ /de yang de yi mtshan nyid bzhed/ /sems ni snga mas byang chub par/ /rigs min phyi mas kyang ni min/ /
10a5(mdo 'grel): mar me'i dpe yi tshul gyis ni/ /zab mo'i chos nyid rnam pa brgyad/ /skye ba dang ni 'gag pa dang/ /de bzhin nyid dang shes bya dang/ /shes dang sbyod dang gnyis med dang/ /thabs mkhas pa la zab pa nyid/ /chos rnams rmi lam 'dra ba'i phyir/ /srid dang zhi bar mi
10a6(mdo 'grel): rtogs pa/ /las med la sogs klan ka yi/ /lan ni ji skad bshad par zad/ /sems can 'jig rten de bzhin du/ /snod kyi 'jig rten ma dag pa/ /de la dag par sgrub pa yis/ /sangs rgyas zhing ni dag pa nyid/ /yul dang sbyor ba can 'di ni/ /dgra rnams las ni 'das
10a7(mdo 'grel): pa dang/ /mi gnas ji bzhin shugs dang ni/ /thun mong ma yin mtshan nyid dang/ /ma chags pa dang mi dmigs dang/ /mtshan ma smon lam zad pa dang/ /de yi rtags dang tshad med pa/ /thabs la mkhas pa rnam pa bcu/ /shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i man
10b1(mdo 'grel): ngag gi bstan bcos mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan gyi tshig le'ur byas pa las/ /skabs bzhi pa'o// //rmi lam na yang chos rnams kun/ /rmi lam lta bur blta la sogs/ /rtse mor phyin pa'i sbyor ba'i rtags/ /rnam pa bcu gnyis dag tu bzhed / /'dzam bu'i
10b2(mdo 'grel): gling gi skye bo snyed/ /sangs rgyas mchod pa'i dge la sogs/ /rnam mang du ni dper mdzad nas/ /rnam 'phel bcu drug bdag nyid do/ /kun mkhyen nyid gsum chos rnams kyi/ /yongs su rdzogs pa bla med pa/ /sems can don yongs mi gtong ba/ /brtan pa zhes ni mngon
10b3(mdo 'grel): bar brjod/ /gling bzhi pa rang stong dag dang/ /stong gnyis gsum dag dper mdzad nas/ /bsod nams mang po nyid kyis ni/ /ting 'dzin yongs su bsgrags pa yin /'jug pa dang ni ldog pa la/ /gzung ba'i rnam rtog so sor de/ /dgu yi bdag nyid ji bzhin yul/ /min
10b4(mdo 'grel): pa'i bdag nyid dag shes bya/ /so so'i skye bo 'phags dbye bas/ /sems can rdzas dang btags yod par/ /rnam rtog 'dzin pa dag tu 'dod/ /de dag so sor dgu bdag nyid/ /gal te gzung don de bzhin med/ /de dag gang gi 'dzin par 'dod/ /de ltar de dag 'dzin pa yi//
10b5(mdo 'grel): ngo bos stong ba'i mtshan nyid do/ /ngo bo nyid dang rigs dang ni/ /lam ni yang dag 'grub pa dang/ /shes pa'i dmigs pa ma 'khrul dang/ /mi mthun phyogs dang gnyen po dang/ /rang gi rtogs dang byed pa dang/ /de yi las bya'i 'bras bu la/ /'jug pa'i phyogs kyi rten can gyi//
10b6(mdo 'grel): rnam rtog de ni rnam dgur 'dod/ /srid dang zhi bar ltung ba'i phyir/ /rtogs pa dman pa nyid dang ci/ /yongs su 'dzin pa med pa dang/ /lam gyi rnam pa ma tshang dang/ /gzhan gyi rkyen gyis 'gro ba dang/ /ched du bya ba log pa dang/ /nyi tshe ba dang sna tshogs nyid/ /gnas dang 'jug la
10b7(mdo 'grel): rmongs pa dang/ /rjes la 'gro zhes bya ba la/ /rnam rtog dgu yi bdag nyid 'di/ /ldog pa'i phyogs kyi rtan can te/ /nyan thos la sogs yid las 'byung/ /'dzin pa dang ni 'dor ba dang/ /yid la byed dang khams rnams ni/ /gsum po dag dang nye 'brel dang/ /gnas dang mngon
11a1(mdo 'grel): bar zhen pa dang/ /chos kyi dngos po btags pa dang /chags pa dang ni gnyen po dang/ /ji ltar 'dod bzhin 'gro nyams la/ /'dzin pa dang por shes par bya/ /ched bzhin nges par mi 'byung dang/ /lam la lam min nges 'dzin dang//
11a2(mdo 'grel): 'gog dang bcas pa'i skye ba dang/ /dngos po ldan dang mi ldan dang/ /gnas dang rigs ni 'jig pa dang/ /don du gnyer dang rgyu med dang/ /phyir rgol ba ni dmigs pa la/ /'dzin pa'i rnam rtog gzhan yin no/ /byang chub la gzhan ston pa dang/ /de yi rgyu ni yongs gtor
11a3(mdo 'grel): dang/ /de thob par chad med pa'i rgyu/ /bsod nams mang po'i mtshan nyid do/ /dri ma zad dang mi skye ba'i/ /ye shes byang chub ces brjod de/ /zad med skye med phyir de dag /go rim bzhin du shes par bya/ /'gog pa med pa'i rang bzhin la/ /mthong zhes bya ba'i laM
11a4(mdo 'grel): gyis ni/ /rnam par rtog rigs ci zhig zad/ /skye med rnam pa ci zhig 'thob/ /gzhan gyis chos rnams kyang yod la/ /shes bya la yang ston pa yi/ /sgrib pa zad par brjod pa gang/ /de la kho bos mtshar du brtsis/ /'di la bsal bya ci yang med/ /gzhag par
11a5(mdo 'grel): bya ba cung zad med/ /yang dag nyid la yang dag lta/ /yang dag mthong nas rnam par grol/ /sbyin pa la sogs re rer ni/ /de dag phan tshun bsngags pa gang/ /skad cig gcig pa'i bzod pa yis/ /bsdus pa de 'dir mthong ba'i lam/ /de nas seng ge rnam bsgyings
11a6(mdo 'grel): pa'i/ /ting nge 'dzin la snyoms zhugs nas/ /rten cing 'brel 'byung lugs mthun dang/ /lugs mi mthun la rtog par byed/ /'gog dang bcas pa'i snyoms 'jug dgur/ /rnam pa gnyis su song 'ong nas/ /'dod par gtogs pa'i rnam par shes/ /mnyam bzhag min pa'i mchis
11a7(mdo 'grel): bzung ste/ /thod rgal du ni snyoms 'jug pa/ /gcig dang gnyis gsum bzhi dang lnga/ /drug dang bdun dang brgyad brgal nas/ /'gog pa'i bar du mi 'drang 'gro/ /mdor bsdus rgyas dang sangs rgyas kyis/ /bstang bas yongs su ma bzung dang/ /dus gsum yon tan med pa dang//
11b1(mdo 'grel): legs pa'i lam ni rnam gsum la/ /gzung ba'i rnam rtog 'di gcig ste/ /sbyor ba'i rnam pa'i sbyor yul can/ /gnyis pa sems dang sems byung rnams/ /'jug pa'i yul can yin bzhed de/ /sems mi skye dang byang chub kyi/ /snying po yid la mi byed dang/ /theg pa dman pa
11b2(mdo 'grel): yid byed dang/ /rdzogs pa'i byang chub yid mi byed/ /sgom dang sgom pa med pa dang/ /de dag las ni bzlog nyid dang/ /ji bzhin don min rnam rtog pa/ /sgom pa'i lam la shes par bya/ /sems can btags pa'i spyod yul dang/ /chos btags pa dang stong min nyid/ /chags
11b3(mdo 'grel): dang rab 'byed bdag nyid dang/ /dngos por byed dang theg gsum dang/ /yon ni dag pa ma yin dang/ /spyod pa rnam par 'khrug pa la/ /'dzin par byed pa dang por ste/ /shes par bya ba bsgrags pa yin/ /sems can btags dang de'i rgyu yi/ /yul tsan de yis rnams 'joms?    
11b4(mdo 'grel): las/ /sgom pa'i lam dang 'brel pa yi/ /mi mthun phyogs gzhan rnam pa dgu/ bdag nyid ji bzhin kun mkhyen ni/ /gsum gyi sgrib pa rnam gsum dang/ /zhi lam de bzhin nyid sogs dang/ /mtshungs par ldan dang mi ldan dang/ /mi mnyam sdug bsngal la sogs dang/ /nyon
11b5(mdo 'grel): mongs rnams kyi rang bzhin dang/ /gnyis su med la kun rmongs la/ /rnam par rtog pa tha mar bzhed/ /yams nad 'di rnams zad nas ni/ /yun ring lon nas dbugs phyin ltar/ /rnam pa kun tu 'gro ba yi/ /bde sgrub yon tan phun tshogs kun/ /rgya mtsho cha la chu bo bzhin//
11b6(mdo 'grel): 'bras bu mchog gis spa ba yi/ /sems dpa' chen po de la ni/ /rnam pa kun tu rten par byed/ /stong gsum skye bo nyan thos dang/ /bse ru'i rtogs pa phun tshogs dang/ /byang chub sems dpa' i skyon med pa/ /bkod pa'i dag pa dper mdzad nas/ /bsod nams mang po nyid
11b7(mdo 'grel): gyis ni/ /sangs rgyas nyid kyi bar med de/ /bar chad med pa'i ting 'dzin / /de ni rnam pa kun nyid/ /'di ni dmigs pa dngos med de/ /bag po dran pa yin par bzhed/ rnam ba zhi 'di la ni/ /rab tu sma rnams rgyun mar rgol/ /dmigs pa la 'thad dang de yin no/ /ngo bo
12a1(mdo 'grel): nyid nges bzung ba dang/ /rnam kun mkhyen nyid ye shes dang/ /dam pa'i don dang kun rdzob dang/ sbyor dang dkon mchog gsum po dang/ /thabs bcas thub pa'i rtogs pa dang/ /phyin ci log ni lam bcas dang/ /gnyen po mi mthun phyogs dang/ mtshan
12a2(mdo 'grel): nyid dang ni sgom pa la/ /smra ba rnams kyis log rtog pa/ /rnam pa kun mkhyen nyid rten can/ /rnam pa bcu drug dag tu bzhed/ /shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i man ngag gi bstan bcos mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan gyi tshig le'ur byas pa las/ skabs lnga pa'o// //sbyin
12a3(mdo 'grel): pa shes rab bar dag dang/ /sangs rgyas la sogs dran dang chos/ /dngos med ngo bo nyid kyis de/ /mthar gyis pa yi bya bar bzhed/ /shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i man ngag gi bstan bcos mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan gyi tshig le'ur byas pa las/ skabs drug pa'o// //
12a4(mdo 'grel): sbyin pa la sogs re res kyang/ /zag med chos kun bsdus pa'i phyir/ /thub pa'i skad cig gcig pa yis/ /rtogs pa 'di ni shes par bya/ /ji ltar skyes bus tho chun rgyun/ /rdog thabs gcig gis bskyod pa na/ /thams cad cig car 'gul ba ltar/ /skad cig cig shes de bzhin no/ /gang
12a5(mdo 'grel): tshe chos dkar thams cad kyi/ /rang bzhin shes rab pha rol phyin/ /rnam smin chos nyid gnas skabs skyes/ /de tshe skad cig gcig ye shes/ /sbyin la sogs pa'i sbyod pa yis/ /chos kun rmi lam 'drar gnas nas/ /chos rnams mtshan nyid med pa nyid/ /skad cig ma ni gcig gis
12a6(mdo 'grel): rtogs/ /rmi lam dang ni de mthong nyid/ /gnyis kyi tshul du mi mthong ltar/ /chos rnams gnyis su med pa yi/ /de nyid skad cig gcig gis mthong/ /shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i man ngag gi bstan bcos mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan gyi tshig le'ur byas pa las/ skabs bdun pa'o// //
12a7(mdo 'grel): thub pa'i ngo bo nyid sku ni/ /zag pa med pa'i chos gang dag/ thob gyur rnam kun rnam dag pa/ /de dag rang bzhin mtshan nyid can/ /byang chub phyogs mthun tshang med dang/ /rnam par thar dang mthar gyis ni/ /snyoms 'jug dgu yi bdag nyid dang/ /zad par bcu yi bdag nyid dang/ /zil gyis gnon
12b1(mdo 'grel): ba'i skye mched ni/ /rab tu dbye bas rnam brgyad dang/ /nyon mongs med dang smon mkhyen dang/ /mngon shes so so yang dag rig/ /rnam pa thams cad dag bzhi dang/ /dbang bcu dang ni stobs bcu dang/ /mi 'jigs pa ni bzhi dag dang/ /bsrung ba chen pa rnam gsum dang/ /dran pa nyer gcig
12b2(mdo 'grel): rnam gsum dang/ /bsnyel ba mi mnga' i chos nyid dang/ /bag chags yang dag bcom pa dang/ /skye la thugs rje chen po dang/ /thub pa kho na'i ma 'dres chos/ /bco brgyad bshad pa gang yin dang/ /rnam pa thams cad mkhyen nyid dang/ /chos kyi sku zhes brjod pa yin/ /nyan thos
12b3(mdo 'grel): nyon mongs med pa'i lta/ /mi yi nyon mongs yongs sbong nyid/ /grong sogs su de'i nyon mongs rnams/ /rgyun gcod rgyal ba'i nyon mongs med/ /sangs rgyas smon nas mkhyen pa ni/ /lhun gyis grub dang chags spangs dang/ thogs pa med dang rtag gi gnas dang/ /dri ba kun la na 'deb
12b4(mdo 'grel): par bzhed/ rgyu ni yongs su smin gyur nas/ /gang dang gang la gang dang ni/ /gang tshe bya ba phan gyur ba / /de dang de la de snang ngo/ /lha yi rgyal pos char phab kyang/ sa bon mi rung mi 'khrungs ltar/ /sangs rgyas rnams ni gyur kyang/ /skal ba med pas bzang mi myong/ /de ltar mdzad pa rgya che'i
12b5(mdo 'grel): phyir/ /sangs rgyas khyab par nges par brjod/ /de nyid zad pa med pa'i phyir/ /rtag pa zhes kyang brjod pa yin/ /mtshan ni sum cu rtsa gnyis dang/ /dbe byad brgyad chu'i bdag nyid 'di/ /theg chen nye bar longs spyod phyir/ /thub pa'i longs spyod rdzogs skur bzhed/ /phyag zhabs 'khor
12b6(mdo 'grel): los mtshan dang du spal zhabs/ /phyag dang zhabs sor dra bas 'brel ba dang/ /phyag ni zhabs bcas 'jam zhing gzhon sha chags/ /'di yi sku ni bdun dag mtho ba dang/ /sor mo ring dang rting yangs sku tsho drang/ /zhabs 'bur mi mngon sbu ni gyen du phyogs/ /byin pa e Na
12b7(mdo 'grel): ya'i 'dra phyag ring mdzes/ /'doms kyi sba ba sbu bsu nub pa'i mchog /pags pa gser mdog pags pa skab pa dang/ /sbu ni re re nas g.yas legs 'khrungs dang/ /zhal mdzod sbus rgyan ro stod seng ge'i 'dra/ /'di yi dbung pa'i mgo zlum thal gong rgyas// 
13a1(mdo 'grel): 'di la'o mi zhim bar ro mchog snang/ /sku ni n+ya gro d+ha ltar chu zheng gab/ /gtsug tor dbur ldan ljags ring mdzes pa dang/ /tshangs dbyangs 'gram pa seng ge'i 'dra dang tshems/ /shin tu dkar dang tshang mnyam thags bzang dang/ /grangs ni bzhi bcu bar
13a2(mdo 'grel): ? tshang ba dang/ spyan ni mthon mthing spyan rdzi ba mchog gi /'dra pa 'di dag sum cu rtsa gnyis mtshan/ /'di la mtshan ni gang gang gi /sgrub par byed pa'i rgyu gang yin/ /de dang de ni rab rdzogs pas/ /mtshan ni 'di dag yang dag 'grub?/ /bla ma skyel la sogs ba dang/ /yang dag
13a3(mdo 'grel): blangs pa brtan pa dang/ /bsdu ba bsten dang gya nom pa'i/ /dngos po sbyin dang bsang bya ba/ /thar par byed dang dge ba ni/ /yang dag blangs pa spel la sogs/ /sgrub byed rgyu yi mtshan nyid de/ /mdo las ji skad 'byung ba bzhin/ /thub pa'i sen mo zangs mdog dang/ /mdog snun mthong
13a4(mdo 'grel): dang sor mo rnams/ /zlum rgyas byin gyis phra ba dang/ /rtsa mi mngon dang mdung pa med/ /long bu mi mngon zhings mnyam dang/ /seng ge glang chen bya dang ni/ /khyu mchog stabs gshegs g.yas phyogs dang/ /mdzes gshegs drang dang 'khril bag chags/ /byi ngor? byas 'dra rim par 'tsham
13a5(mdo 'grel): gtsar dang 'jam dang dag ba'i sku/ /mtshan ni yongs su rdzogs pa dang/ /sku yi kho lag yangs shing bzang/ /gom snyoms pa dang spyan gnyis ni/ /ngag dang gzhon sha can nyid dang/ /sku zhum med dang rgyas pa dang/ /shin tu grims pa'i sku nyid dang/ /yan lag shin tu rnam 'byes dang/ /gzigs
13a6(mdo 'grel): bsgrib med dag pa dang/ /?? zlum skabs phyin ma rnyongs dang/ /phyed ba dang lta ba ni/ /zab dang g.yas phyogs 'khyil ba dang/ /kun nas lta na sdug pa dang/ /kun spyod gtsang dang sku la ni/ /sme ba gnag bag med pa dang/ /phyag ni shing bal ltar 'jam dang/ /phyag ris mdangs yod zab ring
13a7(mdo 'grel): dang/ /zhal ni ha cang mi ring dang/ /mchu ni bimpa ltar ?  med? dang/ /ljags mnyen pa dang srab pa dang/ /dmar dang 'brug gi sgra nyid dang/ /gsung mnyen 'jam dang mche ba zlum/ rno dang dkar dang mnyam pa dang/ byin gyis phra ba shangs mtho dang/ /mchog tu dag pa dag dang ni/ /spyan yangs pa
13b1(mdo 'grel): dang rdzi ma stug/ pad+ma'i 'dab ma 'dra ba dang/ /smin tshugs ring dang 'jam pa dang/ /snum dang spu ni mnyam pa dang/ /phyag ring rgyas dang snyen mnyam dang/ /nyams pa rnam par spangs pa dang/ /dpral pa legs par 'byes pa dang/ dbyes che ba dang dbu rgyus dang/ /dbu skra bung ba ltar gnag dang/ /stug dang
13b2(mdo 'grel): 'jam dang ma 'dzings dang/ /mi bshor dri zhim skyes bu yi/ /yid ni 'phrog par byed pa dang/ /dpal gyi be'u dang bkra shis ni/ /g.yung drung 'khyil pas brgyan pa ste/ /sangs rgyas dpe byad bzang por bzhed/ /gang gis srid pa ji srid bar/ /'gre la phan pa sna tshogs dag /mnyam du mdzad pa'i sku de ni//
13b3(mdo 'grel): thub pa'i sprul sku rgyun mi 'chad/ /de bzhin 'khor ba ji srid 'di'i/ /las ni rgyun mi 'chad par 'dod/ /'gro rnams zhi ba'i las dang ni/ /bsdu rnam bzhi la dgod pa dang/ /kun nas nyon mongs bcas pa yi/ /rnam par byed ba rtogs pa dang/ /sems can rnams de na ji bzhin gyi/ /don dang pha rol phyin drug ??//
13b4(mdo 'grel): sangs rgyas lam dang rang bzhin gyis/ /stong pa nyid dang gnyis zad dang/ /brda dang dmigs pa med pa dang/ /lus can rnams ni ? smin dang/ /byang chub sems dpa' i lam dang ni/ /mngon par zhen pa bzlog pa dang/ /byang chub thob dang sangs rgyas zhing/ /rnam par dag dang nges pa dang/ /sems can don ni tshid?
13b5(mdo 'grel): med dang/ /sangs rgyas rten sogs yon tan dang/ /byang chub yan lag las? rnams ni/ /chud mi za dang bden mthong dang/ /phyin ci log ni spangs pa dang/ /de gzhi med pa'i tshul dang ni/ /rnam par byang dang tshogs dang ni/ /'dus byas 'dus ma byas pa la??/ tha dad? yongs su mi shes dang/ /mya ngan 'das la dgod pa ste/ /chos
13b6(mdo 'grel): kyi sku yi phrin las ni/ /rnam pa nyi shu bdun du bzhed/ /shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i man ngag gi bstan bcos mngon bar rtogs pa'i rgyan gyi tshig le'ur? byas pa la skabs brgyad pa'o// //mtshan nyid yi sbyor ba dang/ /de rab de yi go rim dang/ /de mdza' de yi rnam smin ni/ /don bsdus gzhan de rnam
13b7(mdo 'grel): pa drug /yul ni rnam pa gsum po rgyu/ /sbyor ba bzhi yi bdag nyid dang/ /chos sku phrin las 'bras bu ni/ /don bsdus gzhan te rnam pa gsum/ /'phags pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa man ngag gi bstan pa chos mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan zhes bya ba'i tshig le'ur byas pa rdzogs so// //paN+Di ta go mi 'chi me dang/ lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab kyi 'gyur?
14a1(mdo 'grel): 'phags pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa stong phrag nyi shu lnga pa'i man ngag gi bstan bcos mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan gyi 'grel pa nyi khri snang ba bzhugs// // */ /rgya gar skad du/ pany+tsa bid sha ti sa ha sri
14a2(mdo 'grel): ka Arya pradz+nyA pa ra mi to pa de shA b+hi sa ma yA laM kA ra shAstra sya prit+ti/ bod skad du/ 'phags pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa stong phrag nyi shu lnga pa'i man ngag gi bstan bcos mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan gyi 'grel pa/ bcom
14a3(mdo 'grel): ldan 'das yum shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin ma la phyag 'tshal lo/ /byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ /nyan thos zhi ba tshol rnams kun shes nyid kyis nyer
14a4(mdo 'grel): zhir khrid mdzad gang yin dang/ /'gro la phan par byed rnams lam shes nyid kyis 'jig rten don sgrub mdzad pa gang/ /gang dang yang dag ldan pas thub rnams rnam pa kun ldan sna tshogs 'di gsung pa/ /nyan thos byang chub sems
14a5(mdo 'grel): dpa' i tshogs bcas sangs rgyas kyi ni yum de la phyag 'tshal/ /don gang zhig yin zhe na/ 'phags pa'i gang zag thams cad kyi dbang du mdzad nas thams cad mkhyen pa rnam pa gsum gyi thun mong ma yin pa'i yon tan nye bar dgong pa
14a6(mdo 'grel): sngon du 'gro bas shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ /zhes brjod pa 'di ni de'i mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan gyi man ngag bshad sbyar du bya'o snyam pas rnam par dgrol bar bya'o/ /zhes mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan gyi bshad
14a7(mdo 'grel): pa 'di sbyar bar dam bcas pa yin no/ /ci'i don du zhe na/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen nyid lam/ /ston pas 'di las bshad pa gang/ /gzhan gyis myong ba ma yin ste/ /chos spyod bcu yi bdag nyid kyi/ /mdo don dran pa la
14b1(mdo 'grel): bzhag nas/ /blo dang ldan pas mthong 'gyur phyir/ /bde blag tu ni rtogs pa zhes/ /bya ba rtsom pa'i dgos pa yin/ /zhes de ltar phyag 'tshal ba nye bar bkod pa'i tshigs su bcad par yang dag par mtshon pa'i don 'di yod pa yin no//
14b2(mdo 'grel): zhes gsungs pa yin no/ /ci mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan 'di gzhi bsdus pas sam/ /'on nye gnyen po bsdus pas sam/ de ste rnam pa bsdus pas brgyan du byed pa yin zhes brjod par bya ba yin no/ /de las kyang cir 'gyur zhe na/ /
14b3(mdo 'grel): phyogs dang po ltar na ni 'bad po don du med pa yin te/ mdo sde 'di las mtshan nyid kyi bstan bcos dag las mi smos pa'i gzhi gang yin pa de bshad pa ni med do/ /gnyis pa ltar na rnam par byed pa'i dngos po bsdus pa'i phyir kun nas
14b4(mdo 'grel): nyon mongs pa'i dngos po ma bsdus pas 'di gang gi gnyen po yin pa rtogs par mi 'gyur ro/ /gsum pa ltar na yang rnam pa gzhi med pa tsam zhig bsdus pa'i phyir/ /don rtogs pa med pas cung zad kyang ma bshad pa yin no zhe na/ phyogs
14b5(mdo 'grel): gsum char gyis kyang bsdus pa yin no/ /zhes gsungs pa yin no/ /ci'i phyir zhe na/ nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas dang/ byang chub sems dpa' dang/ sangs rgyas rnams kyi rim pa ji lta ba bzhin thams cad shes ba nyid dang/
14b6(mdo 'grel): lam shes pa nyid dang/ /rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyis mngon par rtogs pa mdza' dag bsdus pa'i phyir ro/ /ji skad du bcom ldan 'das kyis rab 'byor thams cad shes pa nyid ni/ nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas rnams kyi
14b7(mdo 'grel): yin no/ /lam shes pa nyid ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi yin no/ /rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi yin no/ /bcom ldan 'das
15a1(mdo 'grel): ci'i slad du thams cad 'tshal ba nyid nyan thos dang/ rang sangs rgyas rnams kyi lags/ rab 'byor thams cad ni phyi dang nang gi chos rnams ji snyed pa 'di tsam yin la de dag nyan thos dang/
15a2(mdo 'grel): rang sangs rnams kyis shes kyi/ /lam thams cad kyis kyang ma yin la/ rnam pa thams cad du 'ang ma yin pas de'i phyir nyan thos dang/ rang sangs rgyas rnams kyi ni thams cad shes pa nyid ces bya'o/ /bcom ldan
15a3(mdo 'grel): 'das ci'i slad du lam gyi rnam pa 'tshal ba nyid/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lags/ rab 'byor byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis ni/ nyan thos kyi lam gang yin pa dang/ rang sangs rgyas kyi lam gang yin pa dang/
15a4(mdo 'grel): sangs rgyas kyi lam gang yin pa'i lam thams cad bskyed par bya zhing lam thams cad shes par bya la/ de dag kyang yongs su rdzogs par bya zhing/ de dag gis lam gyi bya ba yang bya ste/ smon lam yongs su rdzogs par ma
15a5(mdo 'grel): byas pa dang/ sems can rnams yongs su smin par ma byas pa dang/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing yongs su ma sbyangs pa de dag gis/ yang dag pa'i mdza' mngon sum du mi bya'o/ /de'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ni lam
15a6(mdo 'grel): ni rnam par shes pa nyid ces bya'o/ /bcom ldan 'das ci'i slad du/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi lags/ rab 'byor rnam pa gang
15a7(mdo 'grel): dag dang/ rtags gang dag dang/ mtshan ma gang dag gis/ chos rnams rab tu mtshon pa'i rnam pa de dag dang/ rtags de dag dang/ mtshan ma de dag de bzhin gshegs pas thugs su chud de/ de'i phyir de bzhin gshegs pa
15b1(mdo 'grel): dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi ni/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid ces bya'o/ /zhes gsungs pa yin no/ /de la thams cad shes pa nyid ni chos la 'bad pa'i rten can/ 'bras bu bdag tu rmongs
15b2(mdo 'grel): pa spangs pa can yin no/ /lam shes pa nyid ni theg pa ji lta ba bzhin du nges par 'byung ba dang/ de kho na nyid mngon sum du mi byed pa'i rten can/ sems can bsdus pa sdud pa dang/ sems can yongs su ma smin pa/ yongs su smin
15b3(mdo 'grel): par byed pa dang/ sems can yongs su smin pa rnam par grol bar byed pa'i 'bras bu can yin no/ /rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid ni/ nam mkha' i khams kyi mthas gtugs par sems can gyi don rgyun mi 'chad pa dang/ yang
15b4(mdo 'grel): dag pa'i mdza' rtogs pa dang/ bag chags kyi mtshams sbyor ba spangs pa'i 'bras bu can yin no/ /de lta bas na mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan ni/ gzhi dang gnyen po dang/ rnam pa rnams bsdus pas mngon par rtogs pa yongs su rdzogs
15b5(mdo 'grel): par mdza' dag bstan pa yin no/ /zhes bya ba 'di 'thad pa yin no/ /shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa de gang yin zhes bya ba 'di ni/ brjod par bya'o zhe na/ bshad pa/ shes rab pha rol phyin pa ni/ /dngos po brgyad kyis yang dag bshad/
15b6(mdo 'grel): rnam kun mkhyen nyid lam shes nyid/ /de nas thams cad shes pa nyid/ /rnam kun mngon rdzogs rtogs pa dang/ /rtse mor phyin dang mthar gyis pa/ /skad cig gcig mngon rdzogs byang chub/ /chos kyi sku dang de rnam brgyad/ /sems
15b7(mdo 'grel): bskyed pa dang gdams ngag dang/ /nges 'byed yan lag rnam bzhi dang/ /sgrub pa yi mi rten gyur pa/ /chos kyi dbyings kyi rang bzhin dang/ /dmigs pa dag dang ched dang ni/ /go cha 'jug pa'i bya ba dang/ /tshogs ni nges par 'byung ba ces rnams/ /thub
16a1(mdo 'grel): pa'i rnam kun mkhyen pa nyid/ /mog mog por byed la sogs dang/ /slob ma bse ru'i lam gang dang/ /'di dang gzhan pa'i yon tan gyis/ /phan yon che ba mthong ba'i lam/ /byed pa dang ni mos pa dang/ /bstod dang bkur
16a2(mdo 'grel): dang bsngags pa dang/ /bsngo dang rjes su yi rang ba/ /yid la byed pa bla med dag /sgrub dang shin tu dag pa zhes/ /bya ba 'di ni sgom pa'i lam/ /byang chub sems dpa' mkhas rnams kyi/ /lam shes nyid ni de 'drar bshad/ /shes pas srid la mi gnas
16a3(mdo 'grel): shing/ /snying rjes zhi la mi gnas dang/ /thabs ma yin pas ring ba dang/ /thabs kyis ring ba ma yin nyid/ /mi mthun gnyen po'i phyogs dag dang/ /sbyor dang de yi mnyam nyid dang/ /nyan thos la sogs mthong ba'i lam/ /de 'dra kun shes nyid du 'dod//
16a4(mdo 'grel): rnam pa sbyor bar bcas rnams dang/ /yon tan skyon ni mtshan nyid bcas/ /thar dang nges 'byed cha mthun dang/ /slob pa phyir mi ldog pa'i tshogs/ /srid dang zhi ba mnyam nyid dang/ /zhing dag bla na med pa ni/ /rnam kun mngon rdzogs rtogs pa ste/ /'di ni thabs
16a5(mdo 'grel): mkhas bcas pa yin/ /de yi rtags dang rnam 'phel dang/ /brtan dang sems kun gnas pa dang/ /mthong zhes bya dang sgom pa zhes/ /bya ba'i lam ni so so la/ /rnam par rtog pa rnam bzhi yi/ /gnyen po rnam pa bzhi dang ni/ /bar chad med pa'i ting nge 'dzin//
16a6(mdo 'grel): log par sgrub dang bcas pa ni/ /rtse mo'i mngon rtogs mthar gyis pa/ /rnam gsum rnam bcu skad cig ma/ /gcig gis mngon rdzogs byang chub pa/ /mtshan nyid kyis ni rnam pa bzhi/ /ngo bo nyid longs rdzogs bcas dang/ /de bzhin gzhan pa sprul pa ni//
16a7(mdo 'grel): chos sku mdzad pa dang bcas pa/ /rnam pa bzhir ni yang dag brjod/ /ces bya ba yin no/ /tshig le'ur byas pa bco lngas mdor bsdus pa dang rgyas par bstan pas shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i don bsdus par rig par bya'o/ /ji ltar zhe na/ shes rab pha rol
16b1(mdo 'grel): phyin pa ni/ /dngos po brgyad kyis yang dag bshad ces bya ba nas/ /chos kyi sku dang de rnam brgyad ces bya ba'i bar gyi tshig le'ur byas pa gnyis po dag gis ni mdor bsdus pa yin no/ /de la dngos po brgyad ni 'di yin no/ /'di lta ste/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid dang/ /lam shes pa nyid dang/
16b2(mdo 'grel): thams cad shes pa nyid dang/ rnam pa kun mngon par rdzogs par rtogs pa dang/ rtse mo'i mngon par rtogs pa dang/ mthar gyis pa'i mngon par rtogs pa dang/ sems kyi skad cig ma gcig gis mngon par rtogs pa dang/ chos kyi sku'o/ /sems bskyed pa
16b3(mdo 'grel): dang gdams ngag dang/ nges 'byed yan lag rnam bzhi dang zhes bya ba nas brtsams te/ chos sku mdzad pa dang bcas pa/ rnam pa bzhir ni yang dag brjod ces bya ba'i bar gyi tshig le'ur byas pa bcu gsum gyis ni rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid la sogs
16b4(mdo 'grel): pa don brgyad po de rnams kyi dngos po bsdus te bstan pas rgyas par bshad pa yin te/ de ltar na mdor bsdus pa dang rgyas par bshad pa'i phyir legs par bshad pa yin no/ /don gyi lus rnam par bzhag pa brjod zin to/ /'di phan chad ni don gang la khyad
16b5(mdo 'grel): par can gyi rnam pa gang dang gang gi rab tu dbye ba'i chos gang dag bstan pa de dag gi go rims bsdu ba 'ba' zhig brjod par bya'o/ /de la re zhig /sems bskyed pa ni gzhan don phyir /yang dag rdzogs pa'i byang chub 'dod/ /'on te 'dod pa zhes bya ba 'di ci yin zhe na/
16b6(mdo 'grel): 'di 'dod pa dang de 'dod pas/ byang chub sems dpa' shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la brtson par bya'o zhes mdo nas bshad pa gang dag yin pa 'di yin no/ /'di mtshan nyid ci yin zhes bya ba de nyid mi shes te don gang yin zhe na/ 'di ni stong phrag nyi shu lnga ba
16b7(mdo 'grel): 'di nyid las don du gnyer ba yin no/ /zhes gsungs te/ 'di ltar sems bskyed pa'i dus na byang chub sems dpa' ci nas bdag bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya ba dang gzhan gyi don bsgrub par bya'o zhes de ltar
17a1(mdo 'grel): don du gnyer bar byed ba yin no/ /'o na ni de sems ba skyed par mi 'gyur te/ sems ni yul so sor rig pa'i mtshan nyid can yin la/ don du gnyer ba zhes bya ba ni sred pa yin pas so zhe na/ de ni de ltar bden mod kyi/ 'on kyang 'gro?
17a2(mdo 'grel): ba'i chos la 'dun pa'i mtshan nyid don du gnyer ba yod na sangs rgyas nyid kyi don du sems skyed par byed pas na 'dir rgyus 'bras bu bstan pa yin te/ de ltar na 'dun cing don du gnyer ba'i dge ba'i chos rnams thams cad ces bya ba rjes su mthun par
17a3(mdo 'grel): 'phel bar 'gyur ro/ /yang na don du gnyer ba zhes bya ba ni smon lam yin no/ /sems bskyed pa'i gnas skabs ni don du gnyer ba gtsor gyur pa yin pas na de dang lhan cig spyod pa'i sems bskyed pa la don du gnyer ba bstan pa yin te/ de lta na
17a4(mdo 'grel): yang byang chub sems dpa' rnams smon lam dang ldan pa'i sems bskyed par 'gyur ba zhes bya ba 'thad par 'gyur ba yin no/ /yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub dang gzhan gyi don de yang gang yin zhe na/ de dang de ni mdo bzhin du/ bsdus dang
17a5(mdo 'grel): rgyas pa'i sgo nas brjod ces bya ba gsungs te/ de dang zhes bya ba yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub dang/ de ni zhes bya ba gzhan gyi don to/ /de la de'i bsdus te bstan pa ni 'di yin te/ shA ri'i bu 'di la byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po chos
17a6(mdo 'grel): thams cad rnam pa thams cad du mngon par rdzogs par 'chang rgya bar 'dod pas shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la brtson par bya'o zhes gang gsungs pa yin no/ /de la de'i rgyas par bstan pa ni 'di yin te/ shA ri'i bu 'di la byang chub sems dpa' sems
17a7(mdo 'grel): dpa' chen po mi gnas pa'i tshul gyi shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la gnas te/ sbyin pa po dang sbyin par bya ba dang len pa po mi dmigs ba'i phyir yongs su btang ba med pa'i tshul gyis sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs par bya'o/ /zhes bya ba la
17b1(mdo 'grel): sogs pa gang gsungs pa yin no/ /de la gzhan gyi don gyi bsdus te bstan pa ni 'di yin te/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po phyogs bcu re re zhing gang+gA'i klung gi bye ma snyed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na sems can gang zhig yod pa de dang/ thams
17b2(mdo 'grel): cad phung po lhag ma med pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa'i dbyings su yongs su mya ngan las 'da' bar 'dod pas shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la bslab par bya'o/ /zhes gang gsungs pa yin no/ /de la de'i rgyas par bstan pa ni 'di yin te/ sems can ser sna
17b3(mdo 'grel): can rnams ni sbyin pa la/ tshul khrims 'chal pa rnams ni tshul khrims la rab tu 'god par 'dod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la bslab par bya'o zhes gang gsungs pa yin no/ /de ltar sems bskyed
17b4(mdo 'grel): pa'i mtshan nyid dmigs pa dang bcas pa dang ched du bya ba dang bcas pa brjod nas/ da ni de'i rab tu dbye ba'i mtshan nyid rnam pa nyi shu rtsa gnyis kyi dbang du mdzad pa ni/ de yang sa gser zla ba ma/ /gter dang rin chen 'byung gnas mtsho/ /rdo rje'i sman bshes
17b5(mdo 'grel): gnyen dang/ /yid bzhin nor bu nyi ma glu rgyal po mdzad dang lam po che/ /bzhon pa bkod ma'i chu dang ni/ /sgra snyan chu bo sprin rnams kyis/ /rnam pa nyi shu rtsa gnyis so zhes bya ba gsungs pa yin no/ /de la byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sems bskyed pa dang po 'dun pa dang ldan
17b6(mdo 'grel): pa ni sa lta bu'o/ /shA ri'i bu 'di la byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po chos thams cad rnam pa thams cad du mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar 'dod pas shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la brtson par bya'o zhes gang gsungs pa yin te/ chos thams cad
17b7(mdo 'grel): rnam pa thams cad du mngon par rdzogs par byang chub par 'dod pa ni sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad dang de'i tshogs bskyed pa'i gzhir gyur pa'i phyir ro/ /gnyis pa bsam pa dang ldan pa ni gser bzang po lta bu'o/ /shA ri'i bu 'di la byang chub sems dpa' sems
18a1(mdo 'grel): dpa' chen pos gnas pa med pa'i tshul du shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la gnas te/ sbyin pa dang gtong ba dang yongs su len pa mi dmigs pa'i phyir/ yongs su btang ba med pa'i tshul gyis sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su
18a2(mdo 'grel): rdzogs par bya'o zhes bya ba nas/ de bzhin du chos thams cad mi dmigs pa'i phyir shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs par bya'o zhes bya ba'i bar du gang gsungs pa ste/ pha rol tu phyin pa drug gis bsdus pa'i phan pa dang bde pa'i
18a3(mdo 'grel): bsam pa ni yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub kyi bar du gnas pas na bsam pa yin pa'i phyir ma 'ongs pa dang 'di la rnam par 'gyur ba mi brten pa'i phyir ro/ /gsum pa lhag pa'i bsam pa dang ldan pa ni yar gyi ngo'i zla ba tshes pa lta bu'o/ /des shes
18a4(mdo 'grel): rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la gnas te/ byang chub kyi phyogs kyi chos sum cu rtsa bdun bsgom par bya'o zhes bya ba nas/ mi gtsang ba'i 'du shes dgu bsgom par bya ba'i bar dang/ skyes bu chen po'i rnam par rtog pa brgyad bsgom bar bya ba'i bar dang/ sangs rgyas
18a5(mdo 'grel): kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad bsgom par bya'o zhes bya ba'i bar du gang gsungs pa ste/ dge ba'i chos thams cad rnam par 'phel bar 'gyur bas bsam pa lhag pa yin pa'i phyir lhag pa'i bsam pa zhes bya bas so/ /bzhi pa sbyor ba dang ldan pa ni me lta bu'o/
18a6(mdo 'grel): thams cad shes pa nyid la shes pa dang mthong pas bltas nas 'da' bar 'dod pa dang/ phyir mi ldog pa'i sa la gnas par 'dod pa dang/ lam shes pa nyid yongs su rdzogs par 'dod pa dang rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid rjes su 'thob par 'dod pa'i byang chub
18a7(mdo 'grel): sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la bslab par bya'o zhes gang gsungs pa ste/ thams cad mkhyen pa nyid gsum gyi sbyor ba ni mchog tu gyur pa'i sbyor ba rab tu sbyor ba yin pas na bud shing gi khyad par gyis me bzhin
18b1(mdo 'grel): du gong nas gong du khyad par du 'gro ba'i phyir ro/ /lnga pa sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa dang ldan pa ni gter chen po lta bu'o/ /sems can ser sna can rnams sbyin pa la 'jog par 'dod pa dang/ nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi sbyin pa rnams sems bskyed pa gcig
18b2(mdo 'grel): gis zil gyis mnan par 'dod ba'i byang chub sems dpa' chen pos zhes gang gsungs pa ste/ zang zing gi longs spyod kyi sems can tshang med pa tshim par byed kyang yongs su gtugs pa med pa'i phyir ro/ /drug pa tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang ldan pa
18b3(mdo 'grel): ni rin po che'i 'byung gnas lta bu'o/ /tshul khrims 'chal pa rnams tshul khrims la 'jog par 'dod pa dang/ nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi tshul khrims rnams rjes su yi rang ba dang ldan pa'i sems bskyed pa gcig gis zil gyis mnan par 'dod pa'i byang
18b4(mdo 'grel): chub sems dpa' chen pos shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la bslab par bya'o zhes gang gsungs pa ste/ yon tan rin po che mdza' yas pa thams cad ni de las 'byung ba'i phyir ro/ /bdun pa bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa dang ldan pa ni rgya mtsho chen po lta bu'o/ /
18b5(mdo 'grel): gnod sems dang ldan pa rnams bzod pa la 'jog par 'dod pa dang/ nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi bzod pa rjes su yi rang ba dang ldan pa'i sems bskyed pa gcig gis zil gyis mnan par 'dod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' chen pos shes rab kyi pha rol
18b6(mdo 'grel): tu phyin pa la bslab par bya'o zhes gang gsungs pa ste/ mi 'dod pa thog tu bab pa thams cad kyis 'khrug par mi nus pa'i phyir ro/ /brgyad pa brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang ldan pa ni rdo rje lta bu'o/ /le lo can dag brtson 'grus la 'jog par 'dod
18b7(mdo 'grel): pa dang/ nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi brtson 'grus rjes su yi rang ba dang ldan pa'i sems bskyed pa gcig gis zil gyis mnan par 'dod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' chen pos shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la bslab par bya'o zhes gang gsungs pa
19a1(mdo 'grel): ste/ de ni yid brtan pas mi phyed pa'i phyir ro/ /dgu pa bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang ldan pa ni ri'i rgyal po lta bu'o/ /sems rnam par g.yeng ba rnams bsam gtan la 'jog par 'dod pa dang/ nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi
19a2(mdo 'grel): bsam gtan rjes su yi rang ba dang ldan pa'i sems bskyed pa gcig gis zil gyis mnan par 'dod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' chen pos shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la bslab par bya'o zhes gang gsungs pa ste de ni dmigs pa'i rnam par g.yeng bas mi bskyod
19a3(mdo 'grel): pa'i phyir ro/ /bcu pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang ldan pa ni sman lta bu'o/ /sems can shes rab 'chal pa can rnams shes rab la rab tu 'jog par 'dod pa dang/ nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi shes rab rnams rjes su yi rang ba dang ldan pa'i sems bskyed
19a4(mdo 'grel): pa gcig gis zil gyis mnan par 'dod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' chen pos shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la bslab par bya'o zhes gang gsungs pa ste/ de ni nyon mongs pa dang shes bya'i sgrib pa'i nad thams cad rab tu zhi bar byed pa yin pa'i phyir ro/ /
19a5(mdo 'grel): bcu gcig pa thabs mkhas pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa dang ldan pa ni dge ba'i bshes gnyen lta bu'o/ /dge ba'i sems bskyed pa gcig tsam yang thabs mkhas pas thams cad mkhyen par yongs su bsngo bas mi zad par byed par 'dod pa dang/ sems can
19a6(mdo 'grel): thams cad kyi don gyi phyir dmyal ba dang dud 'gro'i skye gnas dang gshin rje'i 'jig rten gyi sdug bsngal bzod par 'dod pa dang/ bskal pa brgya stong du yang dag par bsags pa'i tshul khrims kyang sems can la bltos nas 'dor par 'dod pa dang/
19a7(mdo 'grel): sangs rgyas kyi rigs su skye bar 'dod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' chen pos zhes gang gsungs pa ste/ de ni gnas skabs thams cad du sems can gyi don yongs su mi gtong ba yin pa'i phyir ro/ /'dir kha cig na re bden pa dang gtong ba dang shes rab
19b1(mdo 'grel): dang nye par zhi ba la brten pa rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi rigs yin no zhes zer ro/ /gzhan dag ni mthong ba'i khams kyis bsdus pa sa la 'jug pa'i sems yin te/ 'di ltar mdo las gang gi tshe sems bskyed pa dang lhan cig skyes pa na byang chub sems dpa' i ? ?
19b2(mdo 'grel): 'gyur ba ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs yin no zhes gsungs pa yin pa'i phyir ro zhes zer ro/ /gzhan dag ni da ltar byung pa'i sangs rgyas thams cad mngon du phyogs par gnas pa'i ting nge 'dzin dang snying rje chen po gnyis ni sangs rgyas kyi rigs yin zhes 'dod?
19b3(mdo 'grel): do/ /la la dag ni sangs rgyas kyis bcas pa'i bslab pa la bya bar 'dod do/ kha cig ni pha rol tu phyin pa drug kha bya'o zhes zer ro/ /gzhan ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi yum ni shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yin la/ yab ni thabs mkhas pa yin pas/ de dag ni
19b4(mdo 'grel): sangs rgyas kyi rigs yin no zhes 'dod do/ /bcu gnyis pa smon lam gyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang ldan pa ni yid bzhin gyi nor bu lta bu'o/ /sangs rgyas kyi sku yongs su bsgrub par 'dod pa dang/ phyogs bcu re re zhing 'jig rten gyi khams mdza' yas pa chos ston pas go
19b5(mdo 'grel): bar byed par 'dod pa dang/ sangs rgyas kyi rigs rgyun mi 'chad par bya bar 'dod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' zhes gang gsungs pa ste/ de ni ji ltar smon pa'i 'bras bu 'grub pa yin pa'i phyir ro/ /bcu gsum pa stobs kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang ldan pa ni nyi ma lta bu'o/ /byang
19b6(mdo 'grel): chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po sems can thams cad kyi bsam pa yongs su rdzogs par 'dod pa la zhes bya ba la sogs pa gang gsungs pa yin no/ /de ni gdul bya'i sems can yongs su smin par byed pa yin pa'i phyir ro/ /bcu bzhi pa ye shes kyi pha rol tu
19b7(mdo 'grel): phyin pa dang ldan pa sgra ba byangs snyan pa lta bu'o/ /stong gsum gyi steng chen po'i 'byung pa chen po bzhi mi rdul phra rab kyi tshang shes bar 'dod pa dang/ de bzhin du sbyin pa 'di ltar byin pa ni 'bras bu chen por 'gyur pa dang/ sbyin pa 'di ltar byin pas ni rgyal rigs shing sA la
20a1(mdo 'grel): chen po lta bu la sogs par skye ba nas/ de ltar mi? dmigs pa'i tshul gyis sbyin pa 'di ltar byin na ni shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs par byed do zhes shes bar 'dod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' chen po zhes bya ba'i bar du gang gsungs
20a2(mdo 'grel): pa ste/ de ni gdul bya 'dun par byed pa'i chos ston par byed pa yin pa'i phyir ro/ /de la sA la chen po zhes bya ba ni mngon par mtshon par bya ba'i dbang phyug dang ldan pa'i phyir ro/ /bco lnga pa mngon par shes pa dang ldan pa ni rgyal po lta bu'o/ /sems bskyed pa
20a3(mdo 'grel): gcig gis phyogs bcu re rer 'jig rten gyi khams mdza' yas pa las yang dag par 'da' bar 'dod pa dang/ stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi chu'i phung po chen po de thams cad lan brgyar sku'i? rtse mos thams cad gtong bar
20a4(mdo 'grel): 'dod cing yang de na gnas pa'i srog chags rnams la mi gnod par 'dod pa dang/ bskal pa bsreg pa'i me kha'i dbugs gcig gis zhi bar bya bar 'dod pa dang/ rnam par 'thor ba chen po'i rlung gi dkyil 'khor sor mo gcig gi rtse mos yongs su
20a5(mdo 'grel): khebs par bya bar 'dod pa dang/ nam mkha' i khams ji tsam pa de thams cad skyil mo krung gcig gis rgyas par dgad par 'dod pa dang/ ri'i rgyal po ri rab la sogs pa'i ri rnams skra nyag ma gcig gis sdams? te gyen du bteg nas 'jig rten gyi khams
20a6(mdo 'grel): gzhal du med par 'phang bar 'dod pa dang/ phyogs bcu re re'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad kyi sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das lha'i mig gis blta par 'dod pa dang/ de rnams las kyang chos bstan pa lha'i rna bas nyan par 'dod pa dang/ sems can thams
20a7(mdo 'grel): cad kyi sems kyi spyod pa shes par 'dod pa dang/ de rnams kyi'ang sngon gyi gnas rjes su dran par 'dod pa dang/ zag pa zad pa shes pa'i mngon par shes pa bsgrub par 'dod cing yang dag pa'i mdza' mngon du mi byed par 'dod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' 
20b1(mdo 'grel): zhes gang gsungs pa ste/ de ni mthu thogs pa med par gzhan gyi don bsgrub ba yin pa'i phyir ro/ /ri'i rgyal po ri rab la sogs pa skra nyag ma gcig gis bcings te 'jig rten gyi khams mdza' yas par 'phen pa la ni ma don par mi bya ste/ bsam gtan
20b2(mdo 'grel): pa rnams kyi dbang 'byor pa ston pa 'di ni bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i chos yin pa'i phyir ro/ /bcu drug pa bsod nams dang ye shes dang ldan pa ni bang mdzod lta bu'o/ /sangs rgyas tshad med pa nyan thos kyi dge 'dun dang bcas pa ji snyed bzhugs pa de dag thams cad
20b3(mdo 'grel): bsod snyoms gcig gis khyed par bya bar 'dod pa dang/ bden pa mthong ba rnams rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras du nas/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub kyi bar la 'jog par 'dod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' chen pos zhes gang gsungs pa yin?
20b4(mdo 'grel): te/ de ni bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs mang po'i bang mdzod lta bu yin pa'i phyir ro/ /bcu bdun pa byang chub kyi phyogs dang mthun pa'i chos dang ldan pa ni lam po che lta bu'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das 'das pa dang ma 'ongs pa dang
20b5(mdo 'grel): da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas kyi yon tan thams cad rjes su 'thob par 'dod pa dang/ chos 'dus byas dang 'dus ma byas rnams kyi pha rol tu phyin par 'dod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' zhes gang gsungs pa ste/ de ni 'phags pa'i gang zag thams cad gshegs
20b6(mdo 'grel): shing rjes su gshegs pa yin pa'i phyir ro/ /bco brgyad pa zhi gnas dang lhag mthong dang ldan pa ni bzhon pa lta bu'o/ /nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyi sngon du 'gro bar 'dod pa dang/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das thams cad kyi nang gi 'khor
20b7(mdo 'grel): du 'gyur bar 'dod pa dang/ byang chub sems dpa' chen po'i 'khor 'thob par 'dod pa dang/ yon rnam par sbyang bar 'dod pa dang/ sbyin pa dang tshul khrims dang sgom pa las byung ba'i bya ba dang/ bkur sti dang rdzas las byung ba dang ldan pa'i bsod nams 
21a1(mdo 'grel): bya ba'i dngos po la sems can rnams dgod par 'dod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' zhes gang gsungs pa yin te/ de ni zung du 'jug pa yin pa'i phyir 'khor ba dang mya ngan las 'das pa gang du 'ang mi ltung bas bde blag tu khyer bar byed pa? phyir
21a2(mdo 'grel): ro/ /de la nang gi 'khor zhes bya ba ni gang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi gsang bar 'jug pa'i ye shes phra bar 'jug pa'i ye shes la rjes su zhugs par gyur pa'o/ /bcu dgu pa gzungs dang spobs pa dang ldan pa ni bkod ma'i chu lta bu'o/ /phyogs bcu'i
21a3(mdo 'grel): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis gsungs pa dang gsung ba dang gsung bar 'gyur ba 'di lta ste/ mdo dang dbyangs kyis bsnyad pa dang lung bstan pa nas/ shin tu rgyas pa dang rmad du byung ba'i bar gang cung zad bstan pa de thams cad thos par 'dod pa dang/
21a4(mdo 'grel): gzung bar 'dod pa dang/ yongs su chub par bya bar 'dod pa dang/ de bzhin nyid du sgrub par 'dod pa dang/ gzhan dag la yang rgya cher ston par 'dod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' zhes bya ba ste/ de ni chu 'dzin pa dang mi zad par 'byin pa dang chos mthun par thos pa dang
21a5(mdo 'grel): ma thos pa'i chos 'dzin pa dang/ bstan pa mdza' thug pa med pa 'byin pa'i phyir/ /nyi shu pa chos kyi dga' ston dang ldan pa ni sgra snyan pa lta bu'o/ /phyogs bcu re re zhing 'jig rten gyi bar yun ring por mun pa mun nag tu gyur pa las kyi 'od kyis snang bar byas
21a6(mdo 'grel): nas de skyes pa'i sems can la sangs rgyas kyi sgra dang/ chos kyi sgra dang/ dge 'dun gyi sgra thos par bya bar 'dod pa dang/ de dag yang dag pa'i lta ba la dgod par 'dod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' zhes gang gsungs pa yin te/ des ni thar pa 'dod pa'i gdul
21a7(mdo 'grel): bya rnams la snyan pa sgrogs pa yin pa'i phyir/ /chos kyi dga' ston yang rnam pa bzhi ste/ 'du byed thams cad ni rtag par so sor rtog pa dang/ zag pa dang bcas pa'i chos thams cad sdug bsngal bar so sor rtog pa dang/ chos thams cad bdag med par so
21b1(mdo 'grel): sor rtog pa dang/ mya ngan las 'das pa ni zhi bar so sor rtog pa'o/ /nyi shu gcig pa bgrong pa gcig pa'i lam dang ldan pa ni chu bo'i rgyun lta bu'o/ /phyogs bcu re rer mdza' yas pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams rnams kyi sems can lang ba dang/ 'o na nga dang/ smon pa dang
21b2(mdo 'grel): gtser? bu dang/ bkres pa dang skom pa la sogs pa dang/ ngan song du ltung ba rnams sdug bsngal de dang de las thar bar byas te mi'i lus 'thob par 'dod pa dang/ de rnams kyang tshul khrims dang ting 'dzin dang shes rab dang rnam par grol ba dang/ rnam par grol ba'i ye shes mthong ba'i phung? po
21b3(mdo 'grel): la dgod par 'dod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' zhes gang gsungs pa yin te/ de ni mi skye ba'i chos la bzod pa thob pas rang gi ngang gis 'jug pa'i phyir dang/ bgrong pa gcig pa nyid ni sa der gtogs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams gzhan gyi don gyi bya ba tha mi dad pa'i phyir ro/ /nyi shu gnyis
21b4(mdo 'grel): pa chos kyi sku dang ldan pa ni sprin lta bu'o/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyod lam bstan par 'dod pa dang/ glang po che'i lta stangs kyis lta bar 'dod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' zhes rgya cher gang gsungs pa ste/ dga' ldan gyi gnas na bzhugs pa kun tu ston pas sems can gyi don bya ba rnam pa thams
21b5(mdo 'grel): cad de la ngag? las pa'i phyir ro/ /sems bskyed pa gsum par mi gtsang pa'i 'du shes dgu bsgom par bya'o zhes gang gsungs pa de ni rnam par bam pa pa'i 'du shes dang/ rnam par 'bus gzhigs pa pa'i 'du shes dang/ rnam par rnags pa ba'i 'du shes dang/ rnam par dmar pa pa'i 'du
21b6(mdo 'grel): shes dang/ rnam par bsngos pa pa'i 'du shes dang/ rnam par zos pa pa'i 'du shes dang/ rnam par 'thor pa pa'i 'du shes dang/ rnam par rus pa pa'i 'du shes dang/ rnam par tshig pa pa'i 'du shes so/ /de la 'tsho ba mthar thug pa'i 'og tu go rim bzhin du spud pa rlung gis khangs pa ltar mtho
21b7(mdo 'grel): bar skrangs shing spobs par 'gyur ba'i phyir rnam par bam pa'o/ /rnam par bam pa nyid ni rnam par bam pa ba'am/ yang na mi mthun pa'i phyir btsog? cing rnam par bam pas na apmA? ta kA te rnam par bam pa ba'o/ /'di ni de lta bu'i rang bzhin can ngo'i lus kyi tshig bla dags yin no/ /de bzhin du
22a1(mdo 'grel): yang bshad pa ni ming ngam btsog pa'i don dag la brjod par bya ba yin no/ /de ni dbyibs la chags pa rnams la lus de'i dbyibs kyi rgud pa ston pa'i phyir 'di bsgom par bya ba yin no/ /'bu rnam pa sna tshogs pa rnams kyis nang du bskyod pas na pi d+hu ta kAM zhes
22a2(mdo 'grel): bya ba rnam par 'bul gzhigs pa ste/ de ni lus kyi mkhregs pa'i dngos po la chags pa la kho de stong gi dngos po nyid bstan pa'i phyir ro/ /gnas tha dad pa nas rnag 'jog pa ni rnam par rnags pa pa ste/ de ni phreng ba dang dri la sogs pa'i dbang las byung ba'i lus kyi dri la chags
22a3(mdo 'grel): pa rnams la lus kyi rma dang 'brel pa'i dri nga ba nyid bstan pa'i phyir ro/ /'di dang de nas khrag 'gyed cing rnam par 'phro la rab tu 'jog pas na rnam par dmar pa pa ste/ de ni rgyan gyis byas pa'i mdzes pa la chags pa la khrag gis spags pa'i mi mthun pa nyid bstan pa'i phyir yin
22a4(mdo 'grel): no/ /rnam par gsal bar sngo bas na rnam par bsngos pa ba ste/ de ni lus kyi kha dog la chags pa la pags pa'i 'dod chags kyi rgud la bstan pa'i phyir yin no/ /khyi dang ce spyang la sogs pas phan tshun du rnam pa sna tshogs par zos pa ni rnam par zos pa pa ste/ de ni nu ma la
22a5(mdo 'grel): sogs pa'i sha rgyas pa la chags pa la sha rgyas pa rnam par 'jig par bstan pa'i phyir yin no/ /lag pa gnyis kyang gzhan du/ rkang pa gnyis kyang gzhan du/ mgo bo yang gzhan du/ sna tshogs par rnam par 'thor bas na rnam par 'thor ba pa ste/ de na yan lag dang nyid
22a6(mdo 'grel): lag gi sgeg pa la chags pa la yan lag dang nying lag rnam par 'thor bar bstan pa'i phyir ro/ /rus pa nyid ni rus pa ba ste 'di ni rus pa sgrel ma dang rus pa gcig gi'ang tshig bla dags te/ de ni so la sogs pa'i rus pa'i 'byor ba la chags pa la lus kyi rus pa'i mi mthun
22a7(mdo 'grel): pa'i dngos po ston pa'i phyir ro/ /rnam par zhu zhing tshig pas na rnam par tshig pa pa ste/ de ni kha dog dang dbyibs la chags pa bags pa dang dbyibs kun tu la bums bston pa'i phyir 'di bsgom par bya ba yin no/ /skyes bu chen po'i rnam par rtog pa brgyad bsgom par bya'o zhes
22b1(mdo 'grel): bya ba ni 'di lta ste/ chos 'di ni 'dod pa chung ba rnams kyi yin gyi/ 'dod pa che ba rnams kyi ni ma yin pa dang/ /chog shes pa dang/ rab tu dben pa dang/ brtson 'grus brtsams pa dang/ dran pa nye bar gzhag pa dang/ mnyam par bzhag pa dang/ shes rab dang ldan pa rnams kyi yin
22b2(mdo 'grel): gyi shes rab 'chal pa rnams kyi ni ma yin pa ste/ skyes bu chen po'i rnam par rtog pa bdun po 'di dag gis gnas brtan maung+gal gyi bu chen po gnas par gyur to/ /bcom ldan 'das kyis kyang maung+gal gyi bu chen po khyod kyis skyes bu chen po'i rnam par rtog pa brgyad po 'di
22b3(mdo 'grel): dag la yang rnam par rtogs shig /chos 'di ni spros pa med pa/ spros pa med pa la kun dga' ba/ spros pa med pa la kun dga' ba'i sbyor ba la rjes su brtson pa'i yin no zhes gsungs so/ /de la 'dod pa chung bas chos bzhi spong ste/ 'di ltar tshul 'chos pa dang/ kha gsag dang/
22b4(mdo 'grel): gzhogs slongs dang/ thob kyis 'jal ba'o/ /de la tshul 'chos zhes bya ba ni 'di na kha cig rnyed pa don du gnyer zhing rnyed pa dang bkur sti dang tshigs su bcad pa 'dod pa sems bltos pa dang bcas pa dang 'brel pas dgon pa pa'am/ phyag dang khrod pa 'am/ stan gcig
22b5(mdo 'grel): pa nas sbyangs pa'i yon tan gzhan gang yang rung ba la nye bar bsten te gnas par gyur pa na/ de 'di snyam du bdag la gzhan dag gis bsnyen bkur byed/ bla mar byed/ mchod pa de byed/ rjod par byed na ci ma rung/ bdag gis kyang rnyed pa dang bkur sti dang tshigs su bcad pa
22b6(mdo 'grel): grub par bya na ci ma rung snyam du sems shing/ de rnyed pa dang bkur sti don du gnyer zhing rnyed pa la sogs pa 'dod pa de tshul de lta bu'i rang bzhin gyi spyod lam byed pa gang yin pa 'di ni tshul 'chos pa zhes bya'o/ /kha bsag ces bya ba ni 'di ni kha cig rnyed pa dang bkur sti la bltos
22b7(mdo 'grel): pa dang bcas pas gzhan dag la 'di skad du khyod ni bdag gi ma ji lta ba de 'dra ba dang/ pha ji lta ba dang/ spun zla ji lta ba dang/ nye du gang yang rung ba dang/ snag gi gnyen mtshams ji lta ba de 'dra ba yin te/ de yang sbyin par bya ste nged kyis kyang khyed la sbyin no/ /nga'i bya ba bgyis te nged kyis
23a1(mdo 'grel): kyang khyed kyi bya'o/ /ngo bo ni thag ring bo nas kyang khyod kyi thang du 'ong zhing kho bo 'dir gnas pa gang yin pa'ang khyed cag nyid kyi don du yin no zhes smra ste/ de de rnams la gces par 'gyur ro/ /rnyed pa don du gnyer zhing byed pa ? ?
23a2(mdo 'grel): bltos pa dang bcas pa sems 'brel pa de gzhan dag la tshul de lta bur kha gsag kun tu smra ba dang/ yongs su smra ba dang/ don du gnyer ba dang/ kha zhus 'brel bar bcas pa dang/ gtsam gsag gi las byed pa gang zhen pa 'di ni kha gsag ces bya'o/ /gzhog
23a3(mdo 'grel): slongs zhes bya ba ni 'di na kha cig so sor brtogs shing rnyed pa la brten nas dngos po de dang de'i rgyu mtshan du las byed pa ste/ khyod kyi lhung bzed 'di ni mdzes so zhe 'am/ chos gos sam/ snam sbyar ram/ mal stan nam/ lde mig skyog po 'am/ khyod kyi yo byad 'di
23a4(mdo 'grel): dang 'di ni bzang po/ /gal te kho bos 'di lta bu zhig rnyed na bcang ba bya ba na/ sbyin pa po'ang rnyed pa dka' o zhes bya ba dang/ gang yang rung ba'i khyim duAng song nas der 'di skad ces kyang smra ste/ khyed kyi 'bras chan 'di ni bzang po yin no/ /sran tshod bzang ngo/ /bla gos
23a5(mdo 'grel): bzang ngo/ /gos bzang ngo/ /khyed kyi bca' par bya ba'am bza' bar bya ba 'di dang 'di ni bzang po yin no/ /sngon chad kyang bdag cag la khyed kyis sbyin par bya ba dang bsgrub par bya bar gyur pa yin la/ kho bo cag kyang khyed kyis byin pa dang bsgrubs pas
23a6(mdo 'grel): dga' bar gyur ba yin na/ da ltar ni khyed cag bdag cag la sbyin par bya ba'am/ bsgrub par bya bar mi sems so zhes smra ba lta bu ste/ de'i so sor brtags nas brkam pa las byung ba'i gzhog slongs kyi las dngos po'i deng de gnyis rgyu mtshan du brjod
23a7(mdo 'grel): pa gang yin pa 'di ni gzhog slong zhes bya'o/ /thob kyis 'jal ba zhes bya ba ni 'di na kha cig rnyed pa don du gnyed ba brnyed pa la sogs pa 'dod pa bltas pa dang bcas pa sems 'drel bas gzhan dag la 'di skad ces khyod kyis ma la yang sbyin par mi bya/ phal?
23b1(mdo 'grel): yang ma yin/ srid mo la yang ma yin/ nye du dang snag gi gnyen mtshams gang yang rung ba gzhan dag la yang sbyin par khyed kyis gang zhig la sbyin par bya ba'am bya ba bsgrub pa yin zhes smra zhing/ /khyim ? zhig tu song nas der mang 'di skad ces khyed kyi khyim du dgra bcom pa
23b2(mdo 'grel): zhugs shing khyed dang dgra bcom pa lhan cig tu brad pa dang/ lhan cig tu 'dug pa dang/ gtam smra bar 'gyur ba ni khyed rnyed pa dang ldan pa'o/ /khyod kyis rnyed pa legs par rnyed do/ /khyed kyis 'byor pa legs par thob bo/ /med rnyed pa'ang don yod pa yin no zhes smra zhing/ de 'di snyam
23b3(mdo 'grel): du 'di dag 'di snyam du bdag cag gi khyim du 'phags pa 'di las ma gtogs par dge sbyong ngam bram ze gzhan ni suAng ma zhugs pas nges par 'phags pa 'di ni dgra bcom pa zhes bya ba yin no zhes bya bar sems na ci ma rung zhes sems pa ste/ rnyed pa don du gnyer ba dang
23b4(mdo 'grel): rnyed pa 'dod pa bltos pa dang bcas pa sems 'brel pa de'i de lta bu'i tshul du gzhan rnams nges par sgrogs pa gang yin pa 'di ni thob kyis 'jal ba zhes bya'o/ /chog shes pa ni rnyed pas rnyed pa 'dod pa spong bar byed pa yin no/ /de la rnyed pas rnyed pa tshol ba zhes bya ba ni 'di na
23b5(mdo 'grel): kha cig rgyal po 'am rgyal po'i blon po 'am bram ze'am khyim bdag gam mchog tu gyur ba gzhan gang yang rung bar gyur pas lhung bzed dam chos gos sam/ snam sbyar ram/ lde mig skyog po 'am/ stan nam/ yo byad gzhan gang yang rung ba byin pa yongs su blangs so zhes gzhan
23b6(mdo 'grel): dag la ston pa dang/ 'di ni bdag la rgyal po che ge mo zhes bya ba'am dam par gyur pa gzhan zhig gis phyi no zhes smra zhing de 'di snyam du 'di rnams 'di ltar de dag kyang re zhig de 'dra bar 'phags pa la sbyin par bya ba'am/ bya ba bsgrub par bya bar sems na/ kho bo cag kyang 'phags
23b7(mdo 'grel): pa la sbyin par bya ba 'am bya ba bsgrub par ci'i phyir mi sems zhes sems na ci ma rung snyam du sems pas/ de'i rnyed pa gzhan gyis rnyed pa gzhan 'dod cing chol ba gang yin pa 'di ni rnyed pas rnyed pa tshol ba zhes bya'o/ /sems bskyed pa'i skabs su mi gtsang ba la sogs pa ci zhig
24a1(mdo 'grel): 'brel zhe na/ sems bskyed pa yongs su mi nyams pa'i chos can nyid shes par bya ba'i don du yin no/ /de yongs su nyams pa'i rkyen ni rnam pa dgu ste/ 'khrig pa'i 'dod chags dang/ 'dod pa che ba dang/ chog mi shes pa dang/ 'du 'jil? mngon
